Important News

Qiongzhou War Comes to an End 92

Cai Tingkai Successfully Mediates Between Both Sides

Inland River Vessels Return to Guangdong, Seagoing Vessels Head to Xiamen

Marine Corps Reorganized by the 19th Route Army

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Chen Jitang's army attacked Qiongzhou, it is heard that the various fortresses in Qiongzhou have mostly been bombed by Chen's air force. It is also reported that the Flying Eagle warship and the Fu'an warship stationed in Qiongzhou have been bombed and sunk. According to a customs announcement, the sinking location of the Flying Eagle warship is between 20 degrees 6 minutes 54 seconds north latitude and 110 degrees 19 minutes 9 seconds east longitude, near Haikou, Qiongzhou. The mast of the warship can be seen regardless of whether the tide is high or low, which has aroused great attention from all parties. The Flying Eagle warship is a national defense weapon and is worth approximately three million yuan. If it is unfortunately sacrificed, it would be a great pity. Cai Tingkai has made great efforts to mediate the dispute between the two Chens. Chen Ce's side has agreed to accept the mediation. Chen Jitang's side was initially tough, but after Chen Zhangfu, the commander-in-chief of the attack on Qiongzhou, and Ding Jixu, the captain of the second air squadron, returned to the province by plane on the 8th to inquire about the war situation, they also expressed their support for reconciliation. Therefore, Chen Jitang had no choice but to agree to the mediation. On the 6th and 7th, Cai Tingkai repeatedly telegraphed Chen Jitang from his hotel in Hong Kong to discuss the resolution of the Qiongzhou matter. On the 6th, he also sent Fan Qiwu to the province to negotiate the terms of mediation with Chen. Chen Jitang then sent Xiang Hanping to Hong Kong to represent him in discussing everything with Chen Ce. All the agreed upon situations were telegraphed to Chen Jitang by Xiang, and Chen then replied agreeing. It is heard that the general solution for the Qiongzhou matter is that the seagoing warships will sail to Xiamen and be dispatched by the 19th Route Army, the inland river fleet will be incorporated into the First Group Army, and the Marine Corps stationed in Qiongzhou will be transferred to Fujian to assist the 19th Route Army in reorganizing and suppressing the communists. This is the principle that both sides have clearly acknowledged. Other ancillary conditions, such as the protection of the current naval personnel and the First Group Army's subsidy for the Marine Corps' military expenses in Fujian, are still under negotiation. As for the Marine Corps' departure expenses, it is heard that they will be raised by the mediators borrowing 100,000 yuan from Qiongzhou. Qiongzhou people in Hong Kong have been holding meetings for days to discuss the loan. As a result, the Qiongya Chamber of Commerce in Hong Kong will bear 30,000 yuan, the Haikou Chamber of Commerce will bear 40,000 yuan, and the remaining 30,000 yuan will be borrowed and advanced by individual Qiongzhou merchants in Hong Kong, guaranteed by a certain bank, and repaid within three months. Regarding the Marine Corps' monthly military expenses, Chen Jitang has agreed to subsidize 100,000 yuan per month, but only for three months. Cai Tingkai is about to go to Fujian and cannot wait any longer. He has recently sent Tan Qixiu and Weng Guiqing to Qiongzhou during the day to lead the Marine Corps to Fujian. Chen Ce will leave Qiongzhou after the Marine Corps leaves and may go abroad for several months of inspection before returning to the country. (July 11)

New Situation in Guangdong and Fujian Suppressing Bandits 93

Luo Binghui's Troops Attack Shizhong and Longyan

Bandit Troops Now Regard the Guangdong Border as the Forefront

Shantou Correspondence: After the Zhanglong communist bandits fled back to southern Jiangxi, it was heard that Chiang Kai-shek was very anxious about the bandit suppression conference in Lushan and was also discussing response plans in Ruijin. After the bandits' meeting, they moved one after another, moving and draining the people's food and cash in the bandit-locked areas. It is heard that the main bandit forces are concentrated in five locations: (1) The central area is Ruijin, Shicheng, Guangchang, and Yudu; (2) The western area is Ningdu, Xingguo, Huichang, and Anyuan; (3) The southern area is Xunwu, Dingnan, Qiannan, Longnan, and Xinfeng; (4) The eastern area is Changting, Liancheng, Ninghua, Longyan, and Yong'an; (5) The northern area is the junction of eastern Jiangxi and northern Fujian. Since June 25th, Luo Binghui's troops from Changting have launched a full-scale attack on Shizhong, Longyan. Longyan has a security team reorganized from the Social Democratic Party, which is said to be led by Fu Bocui. When the communist bandits purged the party a few years ago, they killed thousands of Social Democrats, so Fu Bocui and Luo have an irreconcilable hatred. The Shizhong militia has fought bloody battles with the bandits many times and is very strong, so the Red bandits failed to capture Shizhong when they previously attacked Zhangzhou. However, the bandits have long regarded the Shizhong militia as a thorn in their side. For this reason, they went south from Yongding Jinxi, Daxiaochi, Kuzhu, and Kanshi to attack Shizhong, Longyan. The bandit crowd numbered more than 10,000, and Luo Binghui was in Liancheng and Changting to support the rear. Since the 25th, the Shizhong militia has held out against the bandits for five days. By the 30th, it was already on the verge of collapse and sent Xie Yangqi to Zhangzhou to request assistance from the garrison.

After the 19th Route Army arrived in Fujian, it was waiting for the entire bandit suppression plan to be decided, so it has not yet advanced to Tinglian in western Fujian. Li Yangjing, the commander of the 3rd Army of the Guangdong Army, went to Guangzhou last month and has not returned to the front line to this day, so the divisions and brigades stationed on the Fujian border have also stopped their carriages and are not moving forward. Therefore, the communist bandits were able to advance and retreat calmly. The troops in Shanghang and Yongding counties are in the city, while the bandits are stationed in the mountains in the countryside, and it is strange that they are in the same corner. Currently, Huang Renhuan's division of the Guangdong Army is stationed in Wuping Jiaoling, focusing on southern Jiangxi. Huang Yanzhen's and Huang Zhiwen's divisions are also guarding the Jiangxi border. Ouyang Xinquan's regiment, the deputy commander of the 8th Division, entered Xingning County on July 1, but did not advance to Fujian and Jiangxi. According to news from the Jiangxi border, the Red bandits are densely concentrated in Anyuan Xunwu. Luotang to Anyuan is the first line of defense for the bandits, Junmenling is the second line of defense for the bandits, and the area near Ruijin is the third line of defense. New-style trenches have been built, and tunnels connect the artillery positions. At ordinary times, they force the people to do various defensive works and advise the people to dig cellars to avoid airplanes. There is also a radio station to command military affairs in the five districts, with the intention of resisting the war for a long time. The bandits pay the most attention to the Guangdong side, regarding the Guangdong border as the front and Guangxin and Fuzhou as the rear. They do not value the Nanchang side, so the major battle for bandit suppression in the future should be at the junction of Fujian, Guangdong, and Jiangxi. (June 6)

First Meeting of the Hubei Provincial Political Reorganization 94

Chiang Communicates Three Matters to Instruct County Magistrates

And Issues Ten Questions to be Answered Within Three Days

Hankou Correspondence: The Hubei Provincial Government held the first meeting of the local political reorganization at 8:00 a.m. on the 14th. The attendees included Chairman of the Provincial Government Xia Douyin, the directors of the various departments and committee members, and the county magistrates, the chief of the secretariat section of the Provincial Government, and other people, totaling over one hundred. First, Xia Douyin reported the decision to hold the meeting and introduced the members of the Party and Government Committee who were present, including Yang Yongtai, Zhang Nanxian, He Zhonghan, Qiu, Geng, Peng Jieshi, and other six people. Then, Yang Yongtai conveyed Chiang Commander-in-Chief's handwritten instructions and issued ten questions for the county magistrates to answer, and said that the Commander-in-Chief had great hopes for the county magistrates. Therefore, whether or not this bandit suppression and village cleansing can be successful depends entirely on how the political forces are promoted. We have already informed you all the day before yesterday. Now there are several instructions from the Commander-in-Chief, which I will convey to you all, please pay attention. In addition, the Commander-in-Chief is concerned about the local situation in the counties and has several questions. Please answer them in writing succinctly within three days. Within the major questions, there are several small questions, please answer them separately as well. Then, Zhang Nanxian gave a speech, stating that the Party and Government Committee has a close relationship with the counties. I am representing the committee to attend, and there are several things that you should pay attention to. Articles 7, 12, and 3 of the organizational regulations of the Party and Government Committee are very important. Therefore, during the vigorous bandit suppression and village cleansing, the Commander-in-Chief specially established the Party and Government Committee to assist in handling matters. You must not neglect Articles 123 in the slightest, and everyone should follow them unanimously. The country is currently in a time of crisis, and the responsibilities of the county governments are very important. That is to say, you have very important responsibilities. At this time of life and death, the county magistrates should not be complacent in Wuhan and perfunctorily deal with matters. You must absolutely not have the slightest idea of relaxation or complacency. We must have three conditions for governing: first, we must be honest and upright; second, we must have a plan; third, we must be courageous. To be a county magistrate today is absolutely not to be an official, you must have a spirit of sacrifice and move forward bravely. Then, He Zhonghan gave a speech, stating that to eliminate the communist bandits, we must use the power of organization. The rampant nature of the communist bandits is not because their armed forces are stronger than our party's armed forces, but because their organization is strict. I hope that the county magistrates will strictly organize themselves after returning to their counties, pool their wisdom and efforts, and work together to proceed. Then, Yang Yongtai gave a speech, stating that this bandit suppression by the Commander-in-Chief is different from formal warfare. The bandits are different from formal troops. When the troops come, the bandits go; when the troops leave, the bandits come. Therefore, we must rely on political forces to maintain the recovered bandit areas and prevent them from falling into the hands of the bandits again. Those who are responsible for administrative responsibility, although there are the National Government and the Provincial Government above, the direct implementing agency is the county government. Therefore, the position and responsibility of the county magistrate are very important. The Commander-in-Chief said in his speech the other day that the county magistrate is an "official who is close to the people," that is, what was previously called the parent of the people. What we hope from you is to make good use of political forces and work hard on bandit suppression. Now, from the central government to the local level, everyone must use their full spirit to deal with bandit suppression. You should pay attention to the various items in Article 9 of the organizational regulations of the Party and Government Committee, but the most important are three points: (1) To actively organize the masses; (2) To strengthen self-defense forces; (3) To complete the tools for bandit suppression. After the above three points are completed, not only will village cleansing and bandit suppression be easier to carry out, but it will also be easier to start post-war reconstruction. Then, Qiu gave a speech, saying that to reorganize the local militias, we must have a unified understanding, that is, the party headquarters and the government must also have a unified examination. He also said that the local militias must implement Baojia system and check household registrations as a basic work, so as to avoid complexity and be susceptible to the propaganda and enticement of the communist bandits. After the speech, the meeting was adjourned. They had lunch at the Provincial Government. At 2:00 p.m., the meeting continued. Except for the members of the Party and Government Committee who were on leave, the number of attendees was the same as before. Xia Douyin was still the chairman and designated the Director of the Construction Department, Li Shucheng, to report on the various items decided at the Lushan Conference, and the Construction Department formulated in detail the points that should be implemented based on the Lushan Conference. Then, all the county magistrates made four requests to the chairman for instructions, and Xia answered them one by one. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 p.m., and it was decided that the second meeting would continue at 8:00 a.m. on the 15th, after which it would be closed.

The three items of Chiang's handwritten instructions to the county magistrates and the ten questions issued to the county magistrates for reply are recorded as follows:

A. Three items of handwritten instructions to the county magistrates: (1) Articles 3, 8, 9, 10, 11, 13, and 14 of our party and government's domestic policy are all policies that are most easy to implement in the bandit areas of the counties. If we cannot vigorously implement this policy, then the communist bandits in Hubei will definitely bring disaster to the country and harm it endlessly. I hope that the county magistrates will implement these seven policies to the best of their ability and encourage themselves morning and evening to ensure that they are implemented. (2) To organize various local militias and manage Baojia, it is necessary to take household registration as the basic condition. If household registration cannot be checked clearly, then the various organizations and movements of village cleansing will be ineffective. Therefore, I hope that the county magistrates must personally supervise and check the household registration by rotation. If there are any false or unclear things, the person in charge must be severely punished. The punishment will be imprisonment for minor offenses and execution for major offenses. (3) During the bandit suppression period, everyone in the agencies, starting with the county magistrate, must be militarized. In terms of affairs, such as education and various professions, they must all be militarized. The people in the countryside must be militarized even more. The county magistrates should set a monthly plan for this. For example, within a month, how many villages can have a few thousand or a few hundred people who can be organized and trained for militarization, so that within half a year or a year, how many percent of the people in the whole county can be militarized. By carrying out this way according to schedule, personally supervising and testing, even if it is not as complete as the planned plan, there must be considerable results. Currently, the county magistrates who are handling affairs are suffering from the lack of plans, lack of schedules, and lack of numbers.

B. Questions issued to the county magistrates for reply: (1) Has the household registration of the county been compiled and checked? What month and year was it held? How many households are there? How many people are there? Is this compilation and check accurate, or is it still roughly estimated? What is the compilation and check method based on? Have there been any changes in household registration due to repeated bandit disturbances recently? What is the situation? (2) How many districts are there in the county according to past practice or the current system? Where is the center of the district? (That is, the location of the district office) What are the names of the important towns and villages under the jurisdiction of the district? Is the current district system in line with reality? Are the names of the district towns and villages all used, or are the names of the district forts, capitals, regiments, and armors still used? Below the district, for handling local self-defense or autonomous affairs, is there any existing organization? What is the level and method of its organization? Is this existing organization effective? What is the actual situation? How has the funding for local self-defense and autonomy in the county been obtained in the past? What is the actual situation? (The above questions should be answered separately in simple tables with diagrams) (3) Has the Baojia system been implemented in the county? Is it handled according to the current system or following the old practice? How should the Baojia system in the county be reorganized and implemented in the future? Are there any opinions? (4) Does the county have a local security team? (Or similar to a security team under a different name) Are there police? What is the organizational system? How is its funding obtained? How many people are there? How many firearms are there? And where is the current location? Are there any opinions on the reorganization and training of the county's security team or police? (5) Does the county have local group defenses, teams, and all organizations for people's self-defense? (Such as the Security Corps, the Strong Men Corps, or the Communist Eradication Volunteer Army, etc.) What is the method and actual situation of its organization? Are there any opinions on the planning and training of the people's self-defense organization in the county in the future? (6) What are the names of the officers of the local security team and group defense team, etc.? Are each of them effective? (7) Does the county have city walls? Are they complete and solid? Are there any fortresses, blockhouses, and all buildings for concentrated population equipment and defensive works in the county's towns and villages? How should the county build fortresses and blockhouses in the future, and how should they be implemented selectively by district? Are there any opinions? (8) Does the county have joint defense communication and all electric wire and telephone equipment? Are there any highways that can be used by cars? How should the county's highways be repaired and connected in the future? (That is, connected with the main roads passing through the county) Are there any opinions? (9) What is the past and present situation of the county's suffering from bandits and disturbances? What is the general economic situation of the county's rural areas? What is the county's financial situation? (10) How should the method of bandit suppression and village cleansing in each county be handled to be effective? Each should state practical and feasible opinions. (July 14)

Xu's Troops Recapture Huo Qiu 95

Xu Tingyao Enters the City to Handle Post-War Affairs

The Remaining Bandits are Being Searched and Suppressed

A dispatch from Bengbu reports that Huo Qiu, located in a remote area of western Anhui bordering Henan, has been a bandit-ridden area in its southwestern regions for a long time. It has been occupied by bandits since May 15th, nearly two months ago. The bandit leader Kuang Jixun led the 21st and 25th puppet armies to ravage the local area, causing immense suffering. Xu Tingyao, commander of the First Column of the Right Route Army for Bandit Suppression, led the Fourth Division and the Independent 40th Brigade under Song Shike from Zhengyang to attack Huo Qiu last month, capturing key passes in succession. He then surrounded Huo Qiu. The bandits built defensive works in the city, relying on the terrain to resist stubbornly. According to intelligence from the front, the battle was extremely fierce at noon on the 12th. Although the bandits in the southern countryside of Huo Qiu repeatedly sent reinforcements, they were ultimately unable to succeed because their rear was cut off by the bandit suppression army. The First Aviation Team, stationed in Bengbu and Hefei, dispatched planes in shifts to fly over Huo Qiu city and drop 35-pound bombs on the bandits, killing countless Red bandits defending the city. By the afternoon, Xu's troops had broken through the main force of Kuang's bandits. At 6 p.m., they surrounded the remaining bandits, making it impossible for them to escape. They eventually killed 2,000 bandits, captured 3,000, and seized hundreds of machine guns and mortars, as well as countless rifles. It is said that Kuang was also injured and may be among the prisoners. It is also reported that a puppet Soviet chairman and several puppet regimental commanders were captured. The remaining bandits are currently being searched and suppressed. Xu Tingyao entered Huo Qiu city at 7 a.m. (the 13th). Important military organs here have received Xu's victory report. After Xu's troops recaptured Huo Qiu, they are now planning post-war affairs and are strictly preventing the Red bandits from making a comeback. The post-war measures include: (1) Issuing good citizen certificates to residents who surrender in areas under government control; (2) Issuing return-home certificates to disaster victims in bandit areas and ordering troops to protect them; (3) Providing substantial support to local self-defense militias; (4) Implementing strict blockade of bandit areas to cut off transportation; those who are evil people who have contact with bandits will be shot immediately; (5) Conducting census and implementing rural cleanup; (6) Building roads with engineering corps to facilitate transportation and benefit military operations. (July 14th)

Second Tragedy for Bengbu Aircraft 96

Fighter Plane Crashes into Barracks After Takeoff

Plane Crashes, Catches Fire, Bullets and Bombs Explode

Two Pilots Killed, Seventeen Soldiers Injured

A dispatch from Bengbu reports that during the Fourth Division Commander Xu Tingyao's attack on Huo Qiu, the First Aviation Team stationed in Bengbu and Hefei also dispatched planes to the bandit area to assist in reconnaissance and bombing, achieving remarkable success. On the morning of the 13th, aviation pilot Chen Guannan, believing that Huo Qiu had been recaptured but that most of the bandits were still between Hongjiaji, Yulinpu, and Sanliuji, dropped ten bombs on new fortifications of the bandits at Pokangkou. He then flew back to Bengbu and reported on the capture of Huo Qiu. At 3:40 p.m., he and Wang Baoting, a mechanic from his team, piloted a No. 103 Douglas aircraft, carrying two machine guns and six 35-pound bombs, intending to fly to Huo Qiu and Liu'an to deliver mailbags and drop bombs and shoot at Yulinpu. However, when taking off from the Xiaoshan South Airfield, there was a strong and turbulent southwest wind. The south side of the airfield also had troops drilling. The plane was pulled up off the ground too early, with insufficient speed, and encountered a strong wind blowing from the right wing, causing it to turn to the left and lose speed. The plane tilted and crashed violently into the west end of the Dongyi Barracks. As soon as it crashed, the plane caught fire, and the gasoline burned fiercely. The Dongyi Barracks was garrisoned by the Wang and Tan Regiments of the 25th Brigade of the Ninth Division. Tan's regiment had just finished drilling, and many guards and orderlies were still in the barracks. When the crowd saw the plane crash, they rushed to draw water and fight the fire, while others approached to watch. However, the bombs attached to the wings were ignited by the fire and suddenly four exploded, with a deafening sound. All 500 rounds of machine gun bullets exploded at the same time, instantly injuring seventeen soldiers of the Wang Regiment. Aviation pilot Chen and mechanic Wang were burned, then suffered a terrible explosion, their bodies blown to pieces and reduced to ashes along with the plane, a sight too horrible to bear. When the plane crashed, the continuous explosions of the bombs made the citizens unable to understand the situation, and they suspected a fire. The police bell on Bengbu Mountain also rang loudly. The entire fire brigade of the Public Security Bureau rushed to the rescue upon hearing the news. After the investigation, only the iron shell of the plane remained, and the cylinder was blown several feet away. Under the iron shell, there were still two unexploded bombs. The two machine guns on the plane had been destroyed. Yan Yucong, captain of the First Aviation Team, also came to inspect the scene, but did not dare to retrieve the unexploded bombs. He sent someone to photograph the plane shell for reporting. The names of the soldiers of the 50th Regiment who were injured by the explosion are listed below: Li Jianshu, injured in the left leg and right tibia; Fan Zhendong, injured in the right leg and left tibia; Huang Bin, injured in the back; Zhang Wenzhi, injured in the left tibia; Chen Debiao, injured in the face.

Page 12

Huang Youxing, injured in the right cheek and back; Yang Ru Xue, injured in the right wrist; Wang Xi, injured in the right shoulder; Wu Jiaxiu, injured in the neck; Ren Zhi, injured in the abdomen and left breast; Xue Jianji, injured in the right arm; Huang Jinhuo, injured in the face; Zhang Jisheng, injured in the left tibia; Li Kongfu, injured in the left arm; Wang Zai, injured in the left tibia; Liu Peilin, injured in the head; Gu Huarong, injured in the leg. All seventeen were injured by fragments of bomb shells. However, Wang Zaichao, Wu Jiaxiu, and Ren Zhilan were more seriously injured and may be in danger of death. They have been sent to the Army Hospital for treatment, while the rest are being treated by the health team in this regiment. It is reported that earlier this month, an accident involving a plane from this team resulted in 50 to 60 casualties. This Douglas aircraft, which was burned and exploded, was purchased for 100,000 yuan and destroyed in an instant, so the loss was also very significant. (July 13th)

Local Dispatches

Songjiang 97

Notorious Bandit Yang Guirong Executed by Firing Squad in Shanghai: A bandit was spotted near the Longwang Temple a few days ago. The patrol of the Second Squad of the Waterborne Provincial Public Security Force engaged the bandit in a fierce firefight, wounding him on the spot. He attempted to escape by swimming, but succumbed to his injuries. His body was found in the territory of Jinshan County, in the 66th Tu of the 19th Bao. The local authorities were notified, and after verification, he was buried. At the same time, the notorious bandit Yang Guirong was captured alive. He confessed to robbery during interrogation and was handed over to the District Headquarters, then transferred to the Garrison Headquarters. After reviewing the evidence, which was conclusive, he was sentenced to death in accordance with the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits. It is reported that he was executed by firing squad the day before yesterday. The bandit who was killed was named Li Xingge, and both he and Yang Guirong were from Xuzhou.

Taicang 98

The Case of Huangjing's Abduction of a Fugitive Solved: Sha Shi, the 21-year-old wife of Wang Rongsheng from Huangjing, who possessed considerable beauty, was enticed and abducted earlier this month by Zhu Aifu, who had worked as a mechanic at the local electric light factory. They fled without a trace. Rongsheng reported this to the local Public Security Bureau, requesting an investigation. The Sijiubao Security Corps apprehended Zhu Aifu and Wang Sha Shi together in the residence of a Chen family in Zhoukongqiao the other day, and handed them over to the Fourth Branch of the Public Security Bureau. After a preliminary hearing by Bureau Chief Qiu Gong, the case was deemed to involve judicial matters and was promptly sent to the General Bureau to be handed over to the county for legal proceedings.

Suzhou 99

Water Police Hand Over Four Captured Robbers: Captain Yi of the First Squad of the Seventh Water Public Security Team stationed in Mudu apprehended robbers Zhou Laotu, Zhang Xingfa, and Xue Longbao in the countryside, and seized a robber boat and two firearms. According to Zhou Laotu's confession, he and Xue Longbao robbed Zhu Jida's family in Xihua Xingli Village in April, and he and Zhang Xingfa robbed Qian Xuting's family in Xihua on June 29th. They were handed over to the District Headquarters for interrogation on the 15th.

An American Accused of Encroaching on Public Property: Qian Shunqing, an employee of the Seventh-day Adventist Church in Zhuangjia Bridge Lane, filed a complaint with the District Procuratorate accusing Keith Oden, the American president of the church, and Shen Xiwun and Ren Yuqiao, Chinese employees, of encroaching on public property. Yesterday, the District Procuratorate summoned them for questioning and is awaiting investigation and handling.

A Brawl Between Police and Civilians: More than ten officers from the Second Squad of the Third Company of the Jinxi Police Team, while patrolling in Yujing on the evening of the 14th, saw watermelons planted in a field and wanted to enter the field to pick them. A large dog suddenly ran out and barked at the officers. The dog's owner, Lu Guanshou, came out to chase the dog and verbally insulted the officers. The officers refused to accept this. At that time, Lu Gentu and Zhu Zhifan came out to mediate, but the officers still refused and severely beat the three men. At this time, more and more neighbors gathered in the village and made things difficult for the officers, even leading to a brawl. Seeing the large number of villagers, the officers returned to the team headquarters and, together with all the officers, went to the village armed and arrested more than ten people, including Lu Guanshou, and took them to the team headquarters. Lu Guanshou, Lu Gentu, and Zhu Zhifan were tied up and beaten with iron bars. Lu and Zhu each lost an eye, their leg bones were broken, and they suffered serious injuries to their waists. They were on the verge of death. The villagers were greatly alarmed and filed a petition with the county government on the 15th, requesting a thorough investigation and severe punishment of the officers who caused the trouble.

Wuxi 100

Scorching Weather and Rampant Tiger Cholera: The weather in Xiyi has suddenly become hot in the past three days, and tiger cholera is rampant in the city and countryside, spreading rapidly, which is alarming. It is most common among women and laborers. The day before yesterday, in Donghetou Lane in the city, a total of eleven men and women died of tiger cholera in one day. More than a hundred people a day come to various hospitals for treatment. If preventive measures are not taken soon, the epidemic may spread even more severely, which is frightening. By the evening, residents inside and outside the city were sleeping in the open air, and the streets were full of people. Prisoners in the prisons also died of heat stroke from time to time. County Chief Chen Chuande specially convened a disease prevention meeting of various organs and groups at 3 p.m. yesterday (the 15th) to discuss all preventive measures.

Changzhou 101

A Homicide Occurs During a Play in the Eighth District: A Qingmiao Opera was performed in Jiaxu, Puren Township, Eighth District of Wuyi the other day. Unexpectedly, a fight broke out among the villagers in the theater, injuring many spectators. Subsequently, Cheng Yuanliang and Yin Shenghuo went missing. After searching everywhere without success, a floating corpse was suddenly discovered near the Bian Dan River Car Road Bridge on the morning of the 12th. Yin's father, Bu Qing, went to identify it and confirmed that it was his son, Shenghuo, and that his body was covered with wounds and blood stains. It was assumed that he had been beaten to death and his body dumped into the river. He filed a report with the County Court on the 14th. Chief Prosecutor Yang Kongxi immediately led police officers and clerks to the countryside to investigate.

Zhenjiang 102

Large Amount of Gold and Silver Smuggled and Confiscated: Zhengtianchang Company of Huaining County, Anhui, previously entrusted Taikoo Anqing Shipping to transport 24 bars of red gold, weighing 200 taels, and 21 silver bars, weighing 207 taels, and 46 silver ingots, weighing 501 taels, to Dafeng Hengjin Company in Shanghai. When the ship arrived in Zhenjiang, it was discovered by Zhenjiang Customs, which suspected it was being smuggled out and confiscated it. After various parties proved that it was not being smuggled but that the export time was rushed and customs declaration had not been made, they requested that the Customs release it. It is now reported that the Customs will impose a discretionary penalty for the illegal smuggling of silver bars and silver ingots and allow their return. However, the smuggled gold bars will be detained in accordance with the regulations and, in accordance with the orders of the Ministry, will be awarded to the public as ordinary smuggled goods.

Yangzhou 103

Central Bank Robbed in Broad Daylight: At 12:00 p.m. today (the 14th), five bandits wearing summer cloth and silk long gowns, speaking with a local accent, suddenly came to the Central Bank on Zuojie in this city. They entered the bank under the pretense of exchanging small bills. However, as they entered, two bandits drew pistols and restrained the bank's petitioning police Zhang Qingfang and Liu, threatening them to remain silent. The other three bandits reportedly entered the vault and robbed 20 yuan in silver and 56 yuan in banknotes. They then left and openly walked through the streets with their guns. The Public Security Bureau's First Precinct learned of the incident. Precinct Chief Liao personally led dozens of officers and, at the same time, telegraphed the County Government Public Security Bureau and various sub-stations, ordering the police force and detectives to pursue and arrest the bandits in separate groups and to strictly investigate hotels and bathhouses. A suspect was captured in Xiaojiajing. The other perpetrators have all escaped.

Chief Prosecutor of the Court Changes: Zhu Ronggui, Chief Prosecutor of the Jiangdu County Local Branch Court, was yesterday ordered by the High Court to be transferred to the position of Judge of the Shanghai Local Branch Court. Zhu's vacancy will be filled by Pan Yinting, Chief Prosecutor of the Huzhou Local Court of Zhejiang.

Nantong 104

Public Security Bureau Requests Levy of Passenger Tax: The Nantong County Public Security Bureau requested the levy of a passenger tax due to a shortage of funds. The county government submitted a report to the province for approval. The order received stated that the passenger tax falls within the scope of the business tax and is not allowed to be levied.

Daxi Wheel Hits a Reef and is Damaged: The Daxi Wheel, loaded with 24,000 packages of salt from Haizhou, was sailing to Yangzhou to unload and deliver them to the Gongji Salt Warehouse when it hit a reef near the Eleven Pier Port of Nantong and ran aground. The bottom of the front cabin was cracked for about three feet, and river water poured in, completely dissolving the salt it contained. Water also entered the middle cabin. In order to raise the ship's hull, some salt packages were also discarded. The salt carried by the ship must be taxed after reaching the Twelve Pier. Because of the accident, a report was submitted to the Lianghuai Salt Transport Envoy's Office and the Yangzhou Audit Branch Office for inspection. On the 14th, Commissioner Xie from Yangyu Warehouse and Commissioner Jian from Yangzhou Audit Branch Office, together with Zhou Jianfu, Chairman of the Nantong Salt Merchants Association, went to inspect. It was estimated that the front and middle cabins suffered a total loss of more than 6,000 packages of salt. Although the patching of the leak in the bottom of the Daxi Wheel's cabin was completed, it was stuck in the muddy beach and had to unload the salt packages before it could drive out of danger.

Gaoyou 105

County Government Investigates the Yuanda Public Funds: Yuanda Money Shop in this city went out of business in February of this year. However, it owed more than 20,000 yuan in labor relief funds, which the county government has repeatedly demanded. The shop has ignored this. Chen Shuren, the manager of the shop, suddenly died of illness the other night (the 11th). The county government plans to arrest the shareholders of the shop and force them to pay up.

Huzhou 106

The Scramble for Rice Expands in Huzhou: Since the autumn floods of last year, farmers in various counties of Huzhou have been on the verge of starvation. Coupled with the famine in the spring and summer of this year, the villagers are even more impoverished. Therefore, there have been incidents of rice grabbing recently. Incidents have been occurring continuously in Wuhu, Shuanglin, Lianshi, and Wuzhen. Recently, it has spread to Luoshe in Deqing. Yesterday, a rice merchant from Shanshi transported more than a hundred piculs of white rice to Lianshi. Suddenly, halfway through, the rice was robbed completely. The town reported this to the county government by telephone. The county sent a police team and detectives to maintain order and also sent a team from the First Regiment of the Security Corps to suppress the incident. It is reported that seven rice robbers have been captured.

Pinghu 107

A Water Fight Ensues Over Seized Boats: The troops of Dai, the 36th Brigade of the Lu Army stationed in Pinghu, were ordered to defend the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway. The brigade headquarters was relocated to Jiaxing, and the brigade headquarters entrusted the county Public Security Bureau to seize civilian boats for transportation. Unexpectedly, about dozens of boats anchored in Donghu suddenly cut their mooring ropes and fled together. The Public Security Bureau police learned of this and quickly drove boats to chase after them, shouting for them to stop. The boatmen openly resisted and used boat poles to beat the police. The police also used bamboo poles to fight back. As a result, in addition to recovering a few boats, the rest were escaped.

Xiaoshan 108

Victims of Economic Oppression: In recent years, due to economic hardship, suicides among people in the countryside have been occurring from time to time. On the 13th, a man from Ningbo hired a boat to Qianjiang and suddenly jumped into the Qianjiang River to commit suicide. His body has not yet been recovered. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 14th, a farmer surnamed Sha from Xixing also committed suicide by drowning because his family could not make a living. In Langyu, Xixing, there was a resident named Yu A Yuan who worked as a foreman in a hosiery factory in Hangzhou. He usually liked gambling and would not hesitate to spend a thousand gold pieces. Now, because he was dismissed as a foreman, he could not maintain his family's livelihood and suddenly had the idea of giving up on life. On the night of the 13th, he secretly consumed two bowls of salt in the kitchen and died. His wife, Chen, believing that there was no money for a coffin and burial after her husband's death, also hanged herself on the morning of the 14th.

Taizhou 109

Clashes Between the Zhang and Hu Families Over Boundary Disputes: The Zhang family of Shijing Village in the western countryside of Xianyi and the Hu family of Pingxi Village in this township had a dispute over the boundary of a stream beach, which led to a clan fight between the two sides. A few members of the Hu family were killed by bullets. It is now learned that the case has been mediated by local gentry. The Zhang family paid 2,000 yuan to comfort the families of the deceased Hu family members, and the two sides have reached a reconciliation.

An Assassination Occurs in Shanfeng: He Laoyang, a farmer from Shanfeng in the eastern countryside of Linyi, was assassinated with a sharp knife in his village last night. He suffered more than ten cuts to his head and feet and bled profusely. He died instantly. The next day, his family reported the case to the county government, requesting a strict investigation and arrest of the murderer.

Letter 110

Letter from Ye Yisun, Jing: To the esteemed editor, I have recently read the article "Aftermath of the Tearing of Cheng Jun" in the Songjiang dispatches column of your newspaper on July 14th, which is completely inconsistent with the facts. The case is under investigation and judgment, and I am afraid it will confuse the public. I am writing to request a correction. Sincerely, Ye Yisun, July 15th.

Education News

Important News 111

Recent Distribution of Free Education in Various Counties of Jiangsu

The Sparsest is in the Huai Area, with One School for Every 200 Square Li

The Densest is in Qingpu, Chuansha, and Jiangyin, with One School for Every Eight or Nine Square Li

The Joint Office for the Preparation of Compulsory Education in Various Counties of Jiangsu has always been praised by all parties for its accurate statistics and rapid timing in the investigation and statistics of compulsory education. Since the founding of the Republic, the office has prepared statistical tables of the implementation of free education in all counties, which have been distributed to the counties and reported to the Ministry of Education and the Department of Education for comparison and progress. The Ministry of Education also forwarded them to various provinces and cities for reference and imitation. Now that the 20th year has just ended, the office has completed the preparation of various statistics on compulsory education in various counties during that year. The following is a preliminary excerpt of the comparison of the area of each county occupied by primary schools (including the primary department of primary schools), which can be used to measure the density of compulsory education distribution.

(2) The area of each county is based on the latest investigation and records of the Department of Civil Affairs. (3) The area is in square li. Decimals less than one square li are not used. (4) The primary departments of complete primary schools are also included in the number of primary schools.

(Research) (1) From the above statistics, it can be seen that among the 61 counties in Jiangsu, the average area occupied by each primary school is less than 10 square li in 5 counties, less than 20 square li in 11 counties, less than 50 square li in 21 counties, less than 100 square li in 12 counties, and between 100 and 300 square li in 12 counties. (2) If 9 square li is the standard for a primary school district, then only two counties in the province have achieved universal primary education, three counties are close to universal primary education, and the remaining counties are mostly more than twice the 9-square-li standard, with the highest being more than 30 times (that is, taking 9 square li as the standard for establishing a primary school, two or more than 30 times as many primary schools still need to be added). (3) Under these circumstances, in order to seek the average development of compulsory education in all counties of the province, what kind of policies should the provincial and county educational administrations adopt, and what kind of efforts should be made to achieve success? This is a major issue that can be studied. (4) At present, the funding for compulsory education in various counties is difficult and tight, so it is difficult to expand step by step until there is an increase in funding. (5) Whether the method of distribution and the setting of school districts in the primary schools already established in various counties, regardless of their density, are all based on a thorough and overall plan for the entire county is closely related to the efficiency of primary schools in the promotion of compulsory education. This is also a major issue that can be studied.

Labor University Students Actively Protect the School 114

Another Telegram Sent Nationwide Yesterday

Regarding the petition by Labor University students Gao Zong and others, although the Executive Yuan responded with a temporary closure and referred the restoration plan to the Ministry of Education for deliberation, as reported previously, the Ministry of Education has not responded to the students' submission and petition. The Executive Yuan's referral of the restoration plan to the ministry has also not yielded a response. The Labor University School Protection Committee believes that the Ministry of Education lacks sincerity and intends to sabotage the school. It has sent a telegram nationwide, stating that the students will continue to protect the school with their original determination and requesting assistance from all sectors. The original telegram is as follows:

To newspaper offices, forwarded to the national public: Labor University is unfortunate, repeatedly subjected to violent destruction. Since the Ministry of Education ordered the school to stop enrollment in the 19th year, there has been the tragedy of forced dissolution. Recently, taking advantage of the destruction from the Japanese bombardment, the Ministry suddenly ordered the school to close. Although the Executive Yuan responded to the students, stating that it was a temporary closure and referred the "Outline for the Development of Labor Education and Reorganization of Labor University" to the Ministry of Education for deliberation, the Ministry ignores opposition from all sides and insists on implementing its plan to close Labor University since the 19th year. It has not shown any intention of adopting the founder's restoration plan or the students' petition. Our committee is determined to oppose this consistent policy of destroying labor education. Unless the government makes a clear statement that Labor University will continue to exist, our committee will continue the school protection movement with its original determination, and will not stop until our goal is achieved. We earnestly hope that the national public will rise up and assist us. National Labor University Student School Protection Committee, bowed. You.

First Day of the National Higher Education Problem Discussion Conference 115

The National Higher Education Problem Discussion Conference began yesterday at 9:00 AM at the meeting hall on the 9th floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA. Around six or seventy representatives from various regions registered. Representatives from Jiaotong University, Xiamen University, Ginling Women's College of Arts and Sciences, and Wuchang China University were elected to the presidium. Lu Lin-Sun of Fudan University was the recorder. First, the chairman of the preparatory committee, Jiaotong University President Li Zhao-Huan, reported on the preparation process. Shanghai University President Liu Zhan-En delivered a welcome speech on behalf of the Shanghai Universities Federation. Xu Pei-Huang, Director of the Education Bureau, spoke on behalf of the Municipal Government. Hu Shu-Hua, President of Tongji University, reported on his participation in the National University President Conference in Beijing. Subsequently, Chen Shi of Wuchang China University, Sun Gui-Ding of Xiamen University, Huang Shi-Jin of Zhijiang College of Arts and Sciences, Yang Yong-Qing of Soochow University, and Ms. Wu Yi-Fang of Ginling Women's College of Arts and Sciences reported on the situations of their respective schools. A group photo was taken. The meeting continued at 2:00 PM in the afternoon. Details of each item will be recorded below.

Yesterday's Continued Representatives: Yesterday, the following representatives continued to arrive: Zhang Yun of the Medical College of National Central University, Yan Fu (represented by Zhao Yun-Wen), Chen Xuan-Shan of Great China University, Tang Wei-Zhi of Wuxi National Studies College (represented by Qian Ji-Bo), Chu Fu-Cheng and Shen Jun-Ru of Shanghai Law College, Zhang Su-Min and Xu Pei-Kun of the School of Commerce of National Central University, Wang Jing-Qi, Wang Er, Hong Shao-Liu, Chen Zhen, and Wang Cheng-Yin of National Labor University, He Shi-Mei, He Shi-Mo, and Gu Ke-Jian of Chi Chih College, Ma Wen-Chuo of Yenching University, and others. Additionally, Li Shu-Tian is a representative of Jiaotong University (mistakenly reported as Tangshan College of Engineering yesterday).

Report on Preparations: Yun Li Zhao-Huan reported on the preparations, saying: "Today, the Higher Education Problem Discussion Conference opens. I would like to briefly report on the preparation process. After the September 18th Incident and the crisis in the Northeast, colleagues in the Shanghai education sector felt that the issue of education saving the nation was extremely important. This spring, the Songhu War suddenly broke out, making the relationship between education and the country and society even more urgent. Various issues must be discussed in detail in order to find appropriate solutions and effective measures. Therefore, we initiated the Higher Education Problem Discussion Conference, seeking opinions from presidents of universities, independent colleges, and vocational schools across the country, as well as education experts. The majority supported it, so we are holding a meeting in Shanghai this morning to discuss these issues together. This is a brief overview of the preparation process. I have three hopes for this conference: (1) How should the problems within universities themselves be improved? (2) How should we unite in the future to study the issues of China's survival and the work we should be doing? (3) I hope that the results of this conference can be adopted step by step. The conference will last for three days, which is short, but the issues discussed are very important. Please discuss them in detail, adopting the strengths and discarding the weaknesses, to truly benefit the country and society."

Mr. Liu Delivers Welcome Speech: Yun, Mr. Liu Zhan-En of Shanghai University delivered a welcome speech, saying: "Today, the Shanghai Universities Federation sincerely welcomes representatives from universities outside Shanghai. The weather is so hot, our hearts are even hotter. We are very sorry because we originally proposed to hold the conference last year, but it was not possible due to the September 18th and January 28th incidents and the national crisis. We must thoroughly reform higher education. Many universities are large but unlearned, and some are not large and unlearned. Now we are studying the current situation. What methods should we use to reform higher education? I would like to share my personal views with you: (1) The issue of students' career paths. What is the mission of universities? Currently, students are studying what they will not use and using what they did not study, or not studying or using at all. How should we solve this problem? (2) The issue of curriculum and teaching materials. Currently, there are very few practical textbooks in the country. How can we make teaching materials and textbooks more practical? (3) The issue of teaching methods, that is, the study of the current credit system and academic year system. (4) The issue of moral education. We must earnestly study this issue because many student movements are related to moral education. (5) The issue of funding. National universities are relatively well-funded, but private universities are not. My opinion is that as long as we stop the civil war, there will be a solution. Moreover, the cost of university students is supported by the countryside. How can the 18th-century rural economy support the 20th-century consumption of universities? (6) The issue of faculty. Currently, there are very few people who are truly educating for the sake of education. We must truly educate for the sake of education. I am raising so many questions that cannot be solved in just two or three days. We need long-term unity. We should look at this issue with both a microscope and a telescope, and then the problem will naturally be easily solved."

Xu Pei-Huang's Speech: Today, I am very honored to represent Mayor Wu at the Higher Education Problem Discussion Conference. Regarding the current state of higher education in our country, according to what I have heard, students often register at a certain school and then send a representative to attend classes. This bad system should be corrected. Furthermore, students should focus on practical knowledge and avoid arrogance, thinking that they can do anything after graduating from university. In reality, when they leave school and enter society to find work, they cannot meet the needs of society. If students have ambition and can focus on scientific research, they may become China's Edison or Ford in the future. You are gathered here today to study and discuss the reform of higher education problems, and I am sure that you will have good results and contributions.

Yesterday's Conference Resolutions: The meeting continued at 2:00 PM in the afternoon, chaired by Li Zhao-Huan and Chen Shi. The resolutions are recorded below: (1) Regarding the issue of promoting education (including moral education), (1) The proposal by Wuchang China University that university students should focus on moral education and self-cultivation was resolved to be changed to "Universities should focus on student life guidance," which will be drafted by the Organizing Committee and then submitted to the conference again. (2) The proposal by Jiaotong University to unify the courses taught by part-time faculty at various schools to focus on research areas and increase teaching effectiveness was withdrawn by the proposer. (3) The proposal by Jiaotong University to provide special guidance to freshmen at each school was resolved to be incorporated into the first proposal. (4) The proposal by Great China University to change the university entrance qualification was resolved to request the Ministry of Education to extend the university entrance pre-test for three years. (5) The proposal by Jiaotong University to pay special attention to the level of Chinese language and strictly enroll students during university enrollment was resolved to be passed and implemented at the discretion of each school. (6) The proposal by Wuxi National Studies College to respect Confucianism to rectify people's hearts was resolved to be rejected. (7) The proposal by Great China University to invite specialized scholars to research and investigate higher education issues and reform basis was resolved to organize a specialized committee for drafting and further discussion. The presidium, together with the original proposer Great China University and Liu Zhan-En of Shanghai University, were appointed as members of the specialized committee. At this point, the meeting was extended by thirty minutes to five-thirty. It was decided to continue the discussion tomorrow morning. Due to the excessive heat, the conference time for today and the 17th will be changed from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM, with rest in the afternoon. The original plan for group discussions was changed to university discussions.

Today's Discussion of Various Cases: The conference received a total of 21 proposals submitted by representatives from various regions. In addition to the seven cases resolved at yesterday's conference, the discussion of various cases will continue today as follows: (1) Regarding the issue of advocating education (including moral education), (8) The case of improving the effectiveness of higher education, Fudan University. (9) The case of requesting the government to designate funds to subsidize private universities annually, Fudan University. (10) The case of improving the school system for art schools and music schools, Shanghai Art College. (11) The case of changing the internship period for medical colleges, Hebei Medical College. (12) The case of university teaching issues, Shanghai University. (2) Regarding the issue of curriculum, (1) The case of improving the university curriculum and raising the level of students, Wuchang China University. (2) The case of abolishing the second foreign language as a compulsory subject, Xiamen University. (3) The case of revitalizing national studies to maintain culture, Wuxi National Studies College. (4) The case of popularizing physical education in schools, East Asia Physical Education College. (5) The case of university foundation issues, Shanghai University. (6) The case of establishing a complete and individual professional curriculum in the last two years of university, Great China University. (3) Regarding the issue of faculty treatment, (1) The case of raising the salaries of full-time professors, reducing the number of full-time subjects, and increasing research work to promote scholarship, Jiaotong University. (2) The case of raising the treatment of faculty and staff in private universities, Wuchang China University. (3) The case of implementing the university faculty qualification regulations, Tongji University.

Municipal Government Scheduled Banquet: The Shanghai Municipal Government has scheduled a public banquet at 12:00 noon on the 17th (Sunday) for the National Higher Education Problem Discussion representatives to promote communication.

World Olympic Games 120

Part of the American Swimming Team Determined

His time was 20 minutes, 19 and 1/5 seconds. Compared to other world records, it is as follows:

World Record: 19 minutes, 7.2 seconds, Pu Lu-Gu (Sweden)

Olympic Record: 19 minutes, 51.8 seconds, Pu Lu-Gu (Sweden)

Japanese Record: 19 minutes, 35.2 seconds, Makino Masazo (Japan)

American Record: 20 minutes, 19.2 seconds, Gu La-Bu (USA)

However, the Swedish Pu Lu-Gu, known as the world's treasure, has withdrawn from the Yamu Zhouya Sports Club and will not participate in this competition. Therefore, Japan, with five competitors with times above 19 minutes, may win the championship this time.

The Past and Present of the World Olympic Games (XI) 122

(9) Opening and Closing Ceremonies

Opening Ceremony: The opening ceremony of the Olympic Games is led by the King or President of the host country. The procedure is as follows:

(1) The King or President enters the venue

(2) The national anthem of the host country is played

(3) Representatives and athletes from each participating country enter the venue in order

(4) Members of the International Olympic Committee and the Special Organizing Committee of the host country's Games enter the venue in succession

(5) The chairman of the Special Committee delivers a speech

(6) The King or President announces the opening of the Games with the following words:

"Today is the opening day of the [number] Olympic Games held in [city]. I, in the name of [name], declare the Games open."

(7) Three cannons are fired, the Olympic flag is raised, and pigeons are released

(8) The Olympic anthem is sung

(9) Athletes take an oath with the following words:

"I swear to participate in the Olympic Games in a faithful and sportsmanlike manner, and I am willing to solemnly accept all the regulations concerning competitive sports stipulated in the Games, to perform true art, so that we respect the glory of the country, and at the same time make the art of the world have the greatest glory, I hereby swear."

(10) The Olympic anthem is sung

(11) Athletes leave the venue to begin the competition

Closing Ceremony: The closing ceremony is held in the stadium on the last day of the Games after the competition is over. The President of the International Committee declares the closing with the following words:

"Now that this meeting is closed, I sincerely extend my thanks to the government of [country], the officials of [city], and all the members of this session on behalf of the International Olympic Committee. There is something to announce: The next Olympic Games has been selected to be held in [city] in [year] [month] [day]. In accordance with the mission entrusted to us, we deeply hope that the young people of all countries will come and participate enthusiastically at that time. If all of you gather at this meeting with a pleasant and friendly spirit, then the Olympic Games will truly be united for the benefit of mankind, its glory will shine everywhere, and it will become increasingly enthusiastic, courageous, elegant, and forever illuminate the continents of the world."

After the President reads the closing remarks, five cannons are fired, music is played, songs are sung, and the Olympic flag is slowly lowered. Then, the Olympic flag, which was donated by Belgium in 1920, is handed over to the mayor of the city, who must keep the flag in the city hall until it is transferred at the next Games.

Joint Meeting to be Held Again Today
