International Radio Station Sends Telegram to Minister of Communications 124

Opposing the Secret Contract with Mackay Company

According to the Kuo Wen News Agency, the International Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications, in order to oppose the secret contract with the American Mackay Company, sent a telegram to Minister Huang, which read: "To Minister Huang Junjian of the Ministry of Communications in Nanjing, it has been widely rumored among Chinese and foreign communications circles that your ministry secretly signed a Sino-American wireless telegraph service contract, a Sino-American wireless telephone contract, and a contract to purchase five telephone machines with the American Mackay Company at the end of last month. The motives and conditions are sufficient to endanger China's newly independent international communications business. Due to the complexity of the internal situation, the person in charge of handling the matter strictly kept it secret during the negotiation, and kept it even more secret after the signing. Not only did the colleagues in the national telecommunications industry have no knowledge of it, but even the Telecommunications Department, which is in charge of national telecommunications affairs, did not understand the inside story. If this news is true, it is greatly alarming. All of us have worked hard to participate in the movement to recover China's international communications autonomy in the past four years, and the pioneering construction of the International Radio Station has been completed. We share the hardships and are extremely concerned about it. With a sense of crisis in our hearts, it is difficult to remain silent. We hereby present the foreseeable drawbacks after the signing of the various contracts in detail to your Excellency: (A) Regarding the Sino-American telegraph service contract, (1) Deliberately creating international disputes and damaging China's foreign reputation. According to the matter of opening wireless telegraph services between China and the United States, the Chinese government and the American Wireless Radio Corporation signed a telegraph service contract in November of the 17th year of the Republic of China, with a term of ten years. Section 2 of the contract states, "The Corporation shall transmit all telegrams within its jurisdiction, whether sent to China or relayed by China, through the above-mentioned wireless circuits, unless the sender specifies the routing..." Section 3 states, "The Chinese government shall transmit all telegrams within its jurisdiction, whether sent to the United States or relayed by the United States, through the above-mentioned wireless circuits, unless the sender specifies the routing..."

Article 11 states, "Both parties shall be free to enter into wireless telegraph service contracts with other countries, but shall not violate the provisions of Articles 2 and 3 of this contract." Section 10 states, "...If the two parties cannot reconcile or resolve disputes over this contract, the disputes shall be submitted to arbitration...Both parties shall be obliged to abide by the decision of the dispute if it is unanimously or overwhelmingly supported by the arbitrator...All arbitration costs shall be borne by the losing party..." It is now found that this contract has only been in effect for one year and seven months since it began to be implemented. However, our side suddenly violated the provisions of Article 11 of the contract and signed another contract with the Mackay Company. Using the means of burying bones like a fox to apply it to domestic laws and regulations is enough to invite the slander of an unorganized country. Now it deliberately disregards the constraints of international contracts, knowing that it will inevitably pay for arbitration in the future, and knowing that it will inevitably be in a losing position during arbitration, but it still does so recklessly. What is its deep intention? We don't need to ask, but where will it place our national personality and foreign reputation? Last year, Czechoslovakia was once fooled by the Mackay Company and violated the contract of the joint venture company and signed another telegraph service contract with it. Later, the joint venture company submitted it to arbitration, and the Czech Republic completely failed. The Mackay contract was revoked. The precedent is not far away. Why should our country repeat the same mistakes and bring trouble upon itself? Some say that the person in charge of signing this contract did not consider this. The Mackay Company has issued another statement, undertaking to bear all the responsibilities of losing the arbitration in the future. We sincerely hope that this rumor is not true, because the minds of those in power in our country are not so childish, and the Mackay Company will not use such improper means in the international community to try to expand its business. But if this news is true, then the business ethics of Mackay are another question. However, it regards the government authorities of our country as children, and regards our country's international contracts as child's play, which is inevitably a loss of face for our country. (2) Self-destruction of international telecommunications business and reduction of reporting efficiency. According to the Mackay Company, it originally belonged to the International Telegraph and Telephone Company (I·T·T) system. In China, the organization belonging to the system, the Pacific Water Line Company, the Shanghai Concession Telephone Company, and the Pacific Water Line have monopolized the telecommunications business between China and the United States for decades. It is the backbone organization that infringes upon China's foreign communications sovereignty. After the expiration of the final contract the year before last, our government negotiated to recover the landing rights, which caused a so-called water line negotiation for a while. The company finally relied on its cunning tricks to make the negotiation situation fully complicated, so that it is still a pending case. However, since the completion of the International Radio Station and the opening of the Sino-American wireless circuit, its arrogance has been slightly diminished. Now, if the Mackay contract is established, the two companies will no longer compete in business due to their relationship under the same system. Naturally, the Pacific Water Line will be given the opportunity to pick up the pieces, and the number of reports from the Sino-American wireless circuit will inevitably be drastically reduced or even disappear. Its policy is no different from suicide. When the Chinese government signed a telegraph service contract with the joint venture company in the 17th year of the Republic of China, it carefully studied and investigated it. It finally concluded that the joint venture company and Western Union Telegraph Company are the most prosperous lines in the Americas, and they can maintain the heavy telegrams and deliver them. The reporting efficiency is the best. Therefore, it granted them the right to sign the Sino-American telegraph service contract. As for the Mackay Company, although PostalTekeguaph is used to forward its reports in the Americas, it can hardly use telegraph methods to forward them except in major cities. The low reporting efficiency can be imagined. In addition, due to the simultaneous business competition within PoslalTeleguaph, the drastic reduction or even disappearance of the number of incoming reports between China and the United States is also expected. The business achievements of the International Radio Station, which were created by the hard work of the majority, will be destroyed at once. Let the ambitious destroy the complete international transportation organization established in our country and revive its declining water line business. Is there anything in the world more painful and regrettable than this? (B) Regarding the Sino-American wireless telephone contract, (1) Giving ambitious people the opportunity to monopolize and invade. According to the International Telephone and Telegraph Company, it has long had a precise plan for the invasion of international Pacific telephone communications. After acquiring the Shanghai Concession Telephone Company, its terrible and vicious aggressive ambitions and tactics have been fully demonstrated in the construction of roads across borders and the promotion of business within the complete territory of our country. Now it is signing a Sino-American wireless telephone contract with it, and the scope has been expanded to the whole country. Although both parties are clearly aware that there is no hope for the development of international telephone services between China and the United States in the near future, for our side, this may be an opportunity to purchase a large number of unnecessary machines, while for the other side, it is because of this that it can achieve its dream of monopolizing China's international telephone communications for many years and unveil the prelude to its entire invasion plan. (C) Regarding the contract for ordering telephone machines, (1) It is not needed in the near future. According to international wireless telephone, it is one of the latest telecommunications businesses in the world. It has only been a few years since it was tested and opened for commercial use. However, due to the huge cost and high call charges, it has not yet reached a developed state even in Europe and the United States. Our country should catch up with the emerging businesses in international transportation, but due to the immaturity of industry and commerce, the backwardness of the economy, and the difference in day and night time between China and the United States, this business should only be used for preliminary application tests. Opening for commercial use is not yet the right time. Your ministry, in view of this, purchased telephone equipment when it recently ordered machines from the British Marconi Company to expand the London line and installed them in Shanghai to prepare for the opening of international wireless telephone. In terms of application needs, it is sufficient to meet the needs. As for the wireless telephone sets in Shanghai that are transferred to inland cities, your ministry has also ordered the directly affiliated electrical machinery factory to plan to manufacture them itself. According to estimates, the cost is only more than 10,000 yuan per set. If your ministry believes that this telephone line must be fully equipped at present, it only needs to order the manufacturing factory to rush to manufacture a few branch machines and install them in major cities, which will cost less than 100,000 yuan. In fact, it is enough to meet the full application. Why spend a huge amount of 2 million to build a bed and frame a house, which is not an urgent practical need for machinery? (2) Wasting international reporting fees, making it impossible for the International Radio Station to maintain itself. It is heard that the telephone machines purchased from the Mackay Company this time include a switchboard, priced at 600,000 yuan, and four branch machines, priced at 1.4 million yuan. At a time when the telecommunications budget is exhausted, the operating income of the International Radio Station must of course be used as a guarantee. According to the current operating income of the International Radio Station, it is ordered to be handed over to the Postal Remittance Bureau on a daily basis, designated as a reserve fund for repaying the loan from the Jiaotong Bank and the machine price of the German Fenggen Marconi Company. It is already difficult to make ends meet. Now, it is ordered to bear the price of 2 million telephone machines, which will inevitably lead to the monthly recurring expenses of the International Radio Station, which will not be able to maintain itself, and there will be no way to purchase maintenance materials. The livelihoods of employees are all exhausted, and the radio station's business will be suspended. The above points are all drawbacks that we believe can be foreseen after the contract is signed. Because it harms the country and the power, and traps our country's telecommunications in suicide, we do not hesitate to be verbose and ask for your wise judgment. As for this negotiation and signing of the contract to purchase machinery, it was carried out secretly by the person in charge during Minister Chen's sick leave. It was never made public. It was not reviewed by the Telecommunications Department, which is in charge of national telecommunications affairs, nor was the International Telecommunications Bureau, which is in charge of the country, allowed to contribute opinions, and no telecommunications experts were allowed to conduct research. In addition, the Mackay Company's attempt to sign this contract did not start today. The public condition was that after the contract was signed, a wireless telephone switchboard worth 600,000 yuan would be donated to the Chinese government. This is a fact that all colleagues in the telecommunications industry in our country know. However, in this negotiation and signing of the contract, the company did not fulfill its promise, and the switchboard was still sold to China for 600,000 yuan. Inevitably, it will greatly damage the reputation of your ministry. We are humble and should abide by the warning of not going beyond our position. However, we have personally participated in the difficulty of recovering our country's international communications sovereignty, so our care is greater than that of ordinary people. Even during the Shanghai war, the radio station was threatened by artillery fire and airplanes every day. We still risked our lives to maintain our country's foreign communications and swore to each other that as long as we had a breath, we would coexist with the radio station. This is the natural duty of every citizen, but it cannot be said that it is not driven by the idea of ​​caring for everything. Now, because we have witnessed the devastation of our country's foreign telecommunications business, felt the thorough criticism of public opinion from the outside, and suffered the blame from our conscience from the inside, we, at the beginning of your Excellency's term of office, do not avoid the axe and iron, and plan to ask for your strict attention and present our opinions. We request your Excellency to quickly investigate the inside story thoroughly. If the contract has been signed but has not been approved and filed by the Executive Yuan, please cancel it immediately to maintain the telecommunications administration and force national power. We are extremely eager to await orders. Respectfully, the International Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications.

Song, Cai, and Yang Submitted Bail Again Yesterday in the Niu Lan Case 125

Lawyers Requested Transfer of Jurisdiction

Chen Ying Went to Beijing to Personally Submit the Petition

According to the New Voice News Agency, after Niu Lan and his wife went on a hunger strike, Song Qingling and Cai Yuanpei jointly submitted bail to allow them to seek medical treatment outside. Later, Luo Wengan and Zheng Tianxi resigned, so they both withdrew their bail. Until yesterday, Song Qingling and Cai Yuanpei suddenly prepared bail again in Shanghai, and Yang Xingfo was added as a joint signatory. Lawyers Chen Ying and Feisi also submitted a petition to the court again yesterday, requesting a transfer of jurisdiction. Chen and others took the 11 o'clock night express train to Beijing last night to personally submit the petition to the Beijing court. The bail of Song, Cai, and Yang was also handed over to lawyer Chen to take to the Beijing court. Therefore, the Niu Lan case has undergone another sudden and major change. The news obtained is recorded as follows:

Submitted Bail for the Second Time Song and Cai have recently arrived in Shanghai one after another. Yesterday afternoon, Song, Cai, and Yang discussed the Niu Lan case again. As a result, they believed that Luo's resignation was not for the bail issue. Therefore, for the sake of maintaining humanity, they decided to continue to guarantee Niu Lan and his wife, and immediately wrote a bail, which was submitted to the Nanjing court.

Chen Fei Went to Beijing Yesterday The reporter visited lawyer Chen Ying and his secretary Shao Yuexu and learned that Chen and foreign lawyer Feisi also prepared a petition on behalf of Niu Lan and his wife yesterday, requesting the Supreme Court to transfer the case to the Shanghai branch court for continued trial. Lawyer Chen and Mr. Feisi took the night express train to Beijing at 11 o'clock last night to submit the petition. The bail of Song Qingling and others was also handed over to Mr. Chen to take to Beijing. It is expected to arrive in Beijing this morning.

Original Text of the Petition The lawyers Chen Ying and Feisi petitioned on behalf of Niu Lan and his wife to transfer jurisdiction to Shanghai. The original text is recorded as follows: For the matter of petitioning to transfer jurisdiction to Shanghai, the petitioners were first accepted by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court in Shanghai according to law for the case of being interrogated for endangering the Republic of China. Later, for other reasons, it was changed to be accepted by the Jiangsu High Court. After petitioning to transfer to the Shanghai branch court, it was rejected by the ruling on the 11th of this month. The reason is that Article 22 of the Criminal Interrogation Law states that the competent court refers to the direct superior court in Article 21 of the same law. Therefore, this petition should be made to the Supreme Court. Under the guidance of the court, the petitioners should again request your court to transfer jurisdiction and state the reasons as follows: (1) According to Article 1 of the Implementing Conditions of the Emergency Law for Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China, "Those who commit crimes under the various articles of the Emergency Law for Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China shall be governed by the High Court or its branch court in the first instance, unless otherwise specifically stipulated in this law and other laws." Based on this, it can be seen that if there is a branch court in the crime area, the branch court should manage it in principle. Only when there is no branch court in the crime area should the High Court manage it. If the High Court tries all cases regardless of whether there is a branch court or not, then the four words "or its branch court" are not just for show. (2) According to Article 13 of the Criminal Trial Law, "The territorial jurisdiction of the court shall be determined according to the place of the crime or the domicile, residence, or location of the defendant." The suspected place of the crime and the domicile, residence, and location of the defendant in this case are all within the Shanghai Public Concession, which is under the jurisdiction of the Second Branch of the High Court. (3) According to Article 21 of the Criminal Trial Law, "If the court cannot exercise jurisdiction over the law or facts, or if there are special circumstances that may hinder public security or cause unfairness in the trial, the direct superior court shall transfer the case to another court of the same level as the original court within its jurisdiction." When this case was accepted by the First Branch of the High Court, there were none of the above-mentioned circumstances, and there was no question of transferring jurisdiction at all. The reason for the transfer of jurisdiction at that time was not due to the ruling of the superior court, but due to the request of the military authorities, which was obviously a special reason. Since the military authorities have recognized that they have no jurisdiction, they should immediately restore the original state and send it back to the original trial court for continued acceptance, which is legal. Now it is under the jurisdiction of the High Court, which is not only inconsistent with the principles of law, but also inconvenient for both the court and the defendant in fact, because Beijing and Shanghai are far apart and it takes time to travel back and forth, such as the summoning of witnesses, the investigation of evidence, and the various required procedures such as exercising appraisal and on-site inspection. According to Article 2 of the Criminal Trial Law, "Public officials who implement the criminal trial procedure shall pay attention to both the favorable and unfavorable circumstances of the defendant in the matters under their jurisdiction." It is necessary to transfer it to the Shanghai branch court for continued acceptance. Moreover, the Shanghai branch court does not mean that it has no legal right to accept it. However, due to the circumstances at the time, the defendant had to be handed over to the military authorities, and the trial procedure of this case was temporarily suspended. As for the detention in Beijing, it was originally because the Shanghai war broke out and the distance between Suzhou and Shanghai was close, and there was a risk, so the defendant was sent to Beijing for temporary detention, which was also one of the special circumstances. Now, the military authorities have recognized that they have no jurisdiction, and the Shanghai war has long stopped, and there is no dangerous situation. Then the special reasons that were considered at that time have all disappeared, and there is no need to be detained in Beijing and tried by the High Court. According to law and fact, it should be returned to the Shanghai branch court for continued trial. The petitioner is a literary scholar and his physique was not very strong. After being detained for more than a year, he has suffered infinite hardships physically and felt great stimulation mentally. After repeatedly making legitimate requests and being repeatedly rejected, he is mentally disturbed and unable to comfort himself. He has no choice but to make a final cry of sorrow by going on a hunger strike. The court should pity and understand this kind of foolish and pitiful suffering, and should not regard it as an unreasonable threat. The defendant is not rejecting the jurisdiction of the Chinese court, but is recognizing the right conferred by law to be tried by a legitimate court in order to obtain the protection of Chinese law. Therefore, for the sake of law and humanity, it is appropriate to give the defendant an opportunity to facilitate him to exhaust his ability to attack and defend, so that even if the judgment is guilty, he can be willing to submit without any regrets. According to the provisions of Article 22 of the Criminal Trial Law, we respectfully request your court to consider and approve the transfer of jurisdiction and continue the trial by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court in Shanghai according to law, so as to comply with the statutory procedures. It is a great convenience. As for other various reasons, they have been detailed in the petition submitted to the High Court on June 29, and please call the volume for review and merge the statement. Furthermore, the petitioners have been on a hunger strike since the 2nd of this month, which has lasted for more than two weeks. They are extremely exhausted and difficult to support. Although the court has sent personnel and defenders to persuade them in vain, they are heartbroken. We especially urge you to make a ruling as soon as possible and do not delay. We are extremely frightened and await orders. Respectfully, the Supreme Court, July 14, 21st year of the Republic of China, Petitioner Niu Lan Wang Deli Zeng, Attorney Chen Ying·Feisi.

Ma Yinchu Discusses the Abolition of Taels and the Adoption of the Yuan Currency 127

The lack of uniformity in China's monetary system has long been a major problem for the social economy. The idea of reform has been advocated for a long time. However, due to the silver standard system being chaotic and unsystematic, it is neither a foreign standard nor a silver tael standard. It is neither fish nor fowl, which is deeply regrettable. Considering that a country's legal currency must be stipulated by law, this is not the case with China's silver taels. The purity and color are complex, and the divisions are made locally. Shanghai uses the "gui yuan," Tianjin uses the "xing hua," and Ping uses the "gong gu". As for the institutions, the Ministry of Finance uses the "ku ping", and the Customs uses the "guan ping." All of these are silver taels, which are sufficient to be cited as obstacles to the unification of the national currency, and the most powerful of these is the "gui yuan." If the "gui yuan" can be wiped out in one fell swoop, then the rest should not be a problem.

The motivation for this currency reform is a coincidence. On the one hand, it is due to the excessive confusion of currencies in the past. On the other hand, it is due to the sharp drop in the value of silver dollars, with a new low of six mace and eight fen. The reasons for the sharp drop in the value of silver dollars are no more than the following six: (1) the collapse of the rural economy, (2) the concentration of funds in cities, (3) the seasonal disorder of finance, (4) the decline of urban industry and commerce, (5) the huge storage of cash, and (6) the frequent banditry in the interior. As the market price of silver dollars has repeatedly fallen, it is better for those who hold silver dollars with a higher purity to melt them into silver, as it seems more profitable. This is because calculating the value as silver dollars is not cost-effective. Therefore, the smelting houses have been extremely busy recently, melting as many as 400,000 to 500,000 silver dollars every day. The remaining unmelted silver dollars are mostly second-rate silver dollars, and their purity may be uniform, which is of great benefit to the unification of the purity of silver dollars. There are many kinds of silver dollars. Those circulating in the market include the Mexican Eagle, the Daqing, the Jiangnan, the Beiyang, the Sun Yat-sen, the Yuan Shikai, and there are also Persian silver dollars and Hong Kong silver dollars, etc. The purity of these dollars is uneven. Now, if we abolish taels and adopt the yuan currency, unifying the currency system, the previous silver coins should be strictly regulated. Now, if we can melt away some of the impure silver dollars, we can gradually move towards consistency. The silver dollars currently used are made in the Hangzhou factory. The purity of its products is in line with the statutory requirements, but in terms of weight, there is a difference of 40 yuan for every 100,000 yuan. In the future, when the method of abolishing taels and adopting the yuan is implemented and the legal price of the new currency is determined, the silver dollars will be prepared for minting in Shanghai. This is because the Beijing factory site has been destroyed and the Hangzhou factory has a smaller scale. The Shanghai factory has the mechanical capacity to produce 500,000 silver dollars per day (more than 180 million yuan per year), and it also has machines for minting subsidiary coins, such as silver dimes and copper coins, etc., all of which can be operated by the Shanghai factory. In the future, the purity of the new currency will be 89%, weighing 7 mace and 2 fen in "ku ping," so each yuan of pure silver will be 6 mace 4 fen and 8 hao, plus a minting fee of 6 li, totaling 6 mace 4 fen 6 li and 8 hao in "ku ping." With the statutory price of silver dollars fixed and the silver tael abolished, there will be no more names of silver dollars in the future. People's hearts can be stabilized, and social finance can be greatly stabilized.

The only difficulty in implementing this strategy lies in the attitude of those with vested interests. The reasons held by the opponents are as follows: (1) They fear that the government will seek profit from it. The government has the power to mint silver dollars and stipulate the legal price of silver dollars. Therefore, when minting silver dollars, it deliberately reduces the purity, and the difference between it and the statutory color is the government's profit. (2) Society will suffer from the increase in paper money. Once the silver tael is abolished, the existing silver dollar chips on the market will be insufficient. Then, the opportunity can be taken to issue paper money indiscriminately, which is of great benefit to banks. Otherwise, the chips will feel scarce, and the social phenomenon will be obviously bad. (3) Silver taels can only be abolished after the unification of hard and soft currencies. Today,

Page 14

most banks issue paper money, resulting in a chaotic amount of paper money on the market. The quality of hard currency is already chaotic, and soft currency is like this. Therefore, abolishing taels and adopting the yuan is a major event, and it seems too early to do so. It seems that the above three points are true but not really true. If the government wants to make a profit, it does not have to wait until after the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan. It can also do so when manufacturing silver dollars in the Hangzhou factory. But the government has not done this at this time, so this point is self-defeating. Moreover, the silver dollars must be publicly verified before leaving the factory. Moreover, after the Shanghai factory is established in the future, there will be no problem in starting the furnace for manufacturing under the supervision of the business community and the industrial community, and the political forces will definitely not be affected. Therefore, it is better to take advantage of the decline in silver dollars and the decline in the price of silver dollars, and when many silver dollars are being melted, strive to abolish silver taels. Otherwise, there is no way to prevent the continued melting of silver dollars. If silver taels are abolished, then society will only use silver dollars and no longer use silver. The purpose of converting silver dollars into silver disappears, so there is no need to ban it, and it will stop naturally.

The opponents do not take into account the overall situation. They are afraid that future profit problems will gradually decrease. They see that the future of the bank is getting better and feel unwilling, and are motivated by private interests, so they express their opposition in order to turn the tide. When we observe from a third-party position, this move may be beneficial to banks, but we must know that the only purpose of abolishing taels and adopting the yuan is not for banks, but for the public. Therefore, the interests of the country should be taken as the premise, and it seems that opposition should not be added horizontally.

From the perspective of the money shops, the benefits will of course be lost. Because Shanghai money shops have current accounts, but no foreign accounts. For example, if a depositor deposits with silver dollars, they will convert it into silver taels according to the market price minus 1.25 (one hao and two hu and five) or 2.5, because silver dollars have no interest, so the depositor is also willing to convert it into silver taels, because silver taels have borrowing interest. When withdrawing, it is cost-effective to increase the market price, and profits can be obtained between the inflow and outflow. If the silver tael is abolished, then the money shop will no longer be able to obtain this benefit, and it is appropriate to oppose it. But this is not a big deal. Now there is something even worse than this, that is, the system of depositing and lending to the same industry will not work. Although there are many banks in Shanghai, and all of them have sufficient capital and good credit, their power is far less than that of money shops. That is, daily receipts and payments, such as those related to money shops, must be entrusted to money shops to act as agents. Because money shops have a clearing house for exchanging notes, banks cannot join. Therefore, the amount of money deposited in money shops by banks is as high as 10 million or as low as 5 or 6 million. Because if you want to entrust the money shop to act as an agent for collection and payment, you must first deposit it. This is called interbank deposit. Now, if we implement the reform of abolishing taels and adopting the yuan, then the only weapon of the money shop, the silver tael, will be defeated. The market will uniformly use money dollars and silver dollars, which are rich in banks. Then, all transactions can be done by banks alone, so there is no need to be controlled by the money shop. The money shop's acceptance of bank deposits will of course be cancelled, so interbank deposit will come to an end due to the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan. Once silver taels are abolished, the use of silver dollars will be greatly expanded. Then, banks will receive and pay more frequently, and it is not enough to set up a bank clearing house to settle everything. After the establishment of the clearing house, the debts between banks can be offset by the method of money shop debit notes, which reduces the use of cash and eliminates the trouble of transportation. It can save procedures and avoid risks. From now on, banks can devote all their efforts to business. Moreover, in times of market panic or financial emergency, the need for cash increases sharply, the borrowing interest rate soars, and borrowing is suspended. If there is a clearing house for adjustment, banks can change to using debit notes to clear their deposits and debts. Therefore, the power of the money shop is further reduced. Therefore, to sum up, the money shop will be affected in three ways after the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan: (1) The profit of one hao and two hu and five will be lost. (2) Interbank deposit is cancelled. (3) The bank clearing house is established. The bank joint reserve established by Shanghai banks this spring is the foundation for the future establishment of a clearing house. The debit notes and public treasury certificates issued are set up for the convenience of banks. Therefore, the prototype of the clearing house has been formed, and it is not impossible. However, the power of the money shop will not immediately disappear completely. The money shop's credit notes, which have a good reputation, can still be used in the market. Because the money shop's notes have a term of five days, seven days, and ten days, merchants naturally enjoy using them because of the interest for a few days. As for the odd numbers, banknotes can be used. However, the clearing silver and clearing head silver used by the money shop will inevitably be cancelled due to the implementation of the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan. Because the words "silver tael" are not established at all after the abolition of taels. It is of great benefit to clearing and money shops, because clearing silver must be paid in cash one day later, so the money shop can engage in obtaining one day's interest. If the number is large, calculated on the basis of 366 days a year, it is equal to one year's interest, which is a considerable profit. It is no wonder that the money shop is doing its best to argue for the existence of silver taels. As for the silver taels mentioned in the money shop's reasons for opposition, once abolished, the chips will feel scarce. If silver dollars and foreign dollars are used together, silver can be replaced by foreign dollars, and foreign dollars can be replaced by silver. It can be adjusted. It will not work after the silver tael is abolished. At first, this statement seems reasonable, but after careful examination, it is meaningless. If the power of the two is combined into one after the silver tael is abolished, isn't it one into two and two into one? Its efficiency is fixed, and it is still the same as before. If there are two small bowls of water, if there is less water in bowl A, the water in bowl B can be used to replenish it. Conversely, when there is less water in bowl B, the water in bowl A can be used to replenish it. This is of course a reasonable statement, but we can also combine the water in two small bowls into one large bowl. The amount of water is not reduced at all, and there is only convenience and no difficulty in application. As for banknotes, they will not be issued too much, because the current government strictly limits the issuance of banknotes. 70% of the cash and 30% of the guarantee reserve must be exchanged for 100% of the banknote issuance amount. Moreover, in Shanghai, there are more foreign dollars and less silver. There are 22 million silver dollars and 50 million taels of silver in Shanghai. Since there are already foreign dollars, there is no need to issue more banknotes. Therefore, the abolition of silver taels does not have much impact on the circulation of banknotes. The money shop also said that the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan must be done after the unification of soft currency. This statement is illogical. Who comes first and who comes later, who can make this judgment? The money shop said this, it seems too boring. The purpose of abolishing silver and using the yuan today is to unify hard currency. There is absolutely no reason why hard currency can be unified without abolishing silver taels.

Now, the advantages of abolishing taels and adopting the yuan are briefly described as follows: (1) Fiscal benefits. The various currency problems in the past in finance are mostly due to the conversion of silver taels into foreign dollars, or the conversion of foreign dollars into silver taels. The currency is formed between the inflow and outflow. (2) It will be easier to start reforming the monetary system in the future. Because the silver currency has been unified, it is easy to handle whether to change to the gold standard in the future or gradually adopt the gold standard, which is not as chaotic as in the past, and there is no way to start. (3) Time saving and cost reduction. If silver taels are abolished, the use of silver dollars will be unified, and the procedures will be simplified. There is no need to record both foreign currency accounts and silver tael accounts as in the past. The cost is large and the procedures are complicated. (4) The bank clearing house can be expected to be established. Due to the needs of the times, the clearing house can of course be expected to be established. It is a strange phenomenon in the international community that there is no clearing house in the banking community in the world today. (5) The silver taels in various places can be abolished one after another. Because the exchange rates in other ports in China are based on the Shanghai gui yuan, the Shanghai gui yuan has been defeated, and the silver taels in various places have no place to stand. (6) The Shanghai Mint will definitely start work. After the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan, the demand for silver dollars is urgent, so the Shanghai factory will start work to help the circulation of currency, and the market prices will not be affected.

The New Agriculture Society and Jinan University Jointly Run the New Agricultural Experimental Zone 128

The China New Agriculture Society has been established for three years. The purpose is to develop the rich resources in the Northwest and improve agriculture in the interior, with the goal of increasing the rate of birth and achieving national prosperity and people's affluence. During these three years, Mr. Ma Shaoji, the founder, has been preaching and contacting in many ways, and has achieved considerable results. In the past year, many well-known people have sponsored its progress, such as Zheng Hongnian, Wei Zizhong, Zhang Peinian, Cha Liangzhao, Tao Zhixing, Wang Zhengyi, Chuan Zuoyi, Gao Guizi, Chen Xihan, Ji Zhizhen, and dozens of others. After the Shanghai War, Mr. Ma believed that the work of fundamental national salvation was even more urgent and imminent. He came to Shanghai to set up an office to discuss everything with the sponsors nearby. He had agreed with Mr. Zheng Zhaojue, the president of National Jinan University, a month ago, to establish a reclamation and animal husbandry school centered on production in Suiyuan as a pioneer in the development of the Northwest, and to hand over 1,000 acres of good land donated by overseas Chinese to Jinan University (in Jurong) to the society for operation as a new agricultural experimental zone for improving agriculture. Mr. Zheng returned to Shanghai a few days ago, and Mr. Ma asked Mr. Zheng to review the planned reclamation and animal husbandry school and discuss the steps to be taken. Yesterday, it was decided to first hold the Jurong experimental zone, which will be funded and carried out by Jinan University and President Zheng. As for the reclamation and animal husbandry school, it will also be started after investigating a suitable location. It is reported that Mr. Ma will take President Zheng's letter to Nanjing to contact him in the next few days, and will also accompany Mr. Zhang Zibin, a member of the Agricultural Art Design Committee of the society, to Jurong to conduct a detailed survey in order to draft a plan and start it as soon as possible. It is said that after Mr. Ma's next agricultural plan is realized, the precarious agricultural future of China will be brightened.

Shanghai Gentry Ye Huijun Died Yesterday 129

Mr. Ye Huijun, a Shanghai gentry, suddenly contracted an abdominal tumor on March 9 this year. He was treated for a long time, but it was ineffective. He died suddenly at 1:30 pm yesterday. Mr. Ye lived to be 70 years old and had two sons, seven grandsons and granddaughters. All sectors of society were deeply saddened by the news.

Portrait of Mr. Ye Huijun 130

Mr. Ye had revolutionary ideas. During the Jiawu and Gengzi Wars, the court was corrupt. He organized a gymnastics association and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to gather comrades and seek self-improvement. In the third year of Xuantong, he officially joined the Tongmenghui and secretly planned the revolution with Shen Manyun, Zhu Shaoqi, Chen Yingshi, Li Pingshu, etc., and organized the Patriotic Association and the National Chamber of Commerce Federation. During the battle on September 13 of that year, he personally supervised the members of the regiment and attacked the Gaochangmiao Manufacturing Bureau. After a day and night of fierce fighting, the sea was recovered. Later, the Shanghai Military Governor's Office was established, and Mr. Ye served as the temporary military and political commander. In the first year of the Republic of China, he followed the Premier to the capital and served as the police chief of the Presidential Palace. When Yuan Shikai proclaimed himself emperor, he once bought Mr. Ye for 5,000 gold. He fled to Fusang in the east and took the opportunity to investigate the industry and commerce of that country. After Yuan's defeat, he returned to Shanghai and engaged in local undertakings. He successively served as the director of the Commodity Exhibition Hall, the director of the County Chamber of Commerce, the president of the Miscellaneous Grain Association, the director of the Soybean and Rice Industry, the councilor of the Shanghai Special City Council, the member of the City Government Construction Discussion Committee, and the executive member of the General Chamber of Commerce. In short, throughout his life, he devoted himself to the country and the local area. His death is also a misfortune for the people of Shanghai.

Dr. Jin Jingyang Passed Away 131

Dr. Jin Jingyang (Dr. See Moi King) had profound knowledge and clear talent, and was one of the few figures in the political and academic circles of modern times. He served as the director of education in China Public School, Political University, and Guanghua University. The students obeyed him. He also served as the counselor of the Ministry of Railways and the director of the Finance Department, and was known for his integrity and ability. He was especially unwilling to compromise. He wrote books such as "Fundraising to Revitalize the Country's Party and Government Commentary." Now he has died of a long illness

Portrait of Dr. Jin Jingyang 132

at 6:30 am yesterday. Chinese and foreign people were deeply saddened and regretted. Dr. Jin graduated from Kiel University in Germany and obtained a doctorate with a thesis on the reorganization of China's monetary system. At that time, he was respected by the world.

The County Security Corps Special Training Class Started Yesterday 133

The Shanghai County Security Corps planned to set up a special training class. After the active preparation of Xu Yi, the teacher of the class, the opening ceremony was held in the auditorium of the county government yesterday. More than 100 people attended the meeting, including representatives of the county party department, directors of various bureaus in the county, directors and heads of districts, chiefs of various public security bureaus, representatives of various agencies, and all the students. The chairman, Yan, who is also the general head, reported on the preparation process and delivered a speech (recorded later). Then, Peng Liren, the representative of the county party department, Shi She, the director of the education bureau, and Wu Shifang, the director of the first district, successively gave speeches and took photos. Then, the representatives visited the classrooms and dormitories. The internal layout was clean and tidy, and they were praised. It is heard that the students admitted to the class were selected by the district regiments from the outstanding members of the current Jia Pai (甲牌) leader and deputy captain, so they were full of energy and the level was neat. The instructors, Lu Zhongyu, Fu Dianying, Ge Xiusheng, and Yan Jingtang, all have considerable experience in academic subjects. The training speech of Yan, the general head, is recorded as follows: Most of the security groups in various places adopt the employment system, which is inconsistent with the current security group law. The intention of the security group law is to have the people defend themselves, that is, the people defend themselves, not to have others defend us by employing mercenaries. It is still "defending others" rather than "self-defense." However, if the people are to defend themselves, they must have self-defense, organization and self-defense capabilities. To have an organization, it is necessary to focus on investigating the population and organizing the strong men. However, after the organization, if they are not given skill and knowledge training, they will still not be capable. This county followed the provincial order and completed the organization work in a practical manner before the deadline. The continued work is to start training. However, the number of members is large, and it is impossible to concentrate the training. There are not so many people in the government to teach them individually. Therefore, the Provincial Security Committee has stipulated the method of special training classes, drawing out a few outstanding members from each district and coming to the county for centralized training. You must exercise your responsibility, which is very important. You will not only be excellent and dedicated members in the future, but also go back to each district to train other members. In other words, you are the cadres of the security groups in each district. Whether the purpose of the people's self-defense can be achieved and whether there is real self-defense power depends on whether you can work hard during your studies and after you go out. Although the training and internship period is only six months, I have clearly instructed all the instructors to do it in a down-to-earth and serious manner. Since you are here to receive military training, you should strictly obey discipline and not relax at all. The weather is very hot now. You have to go to the drill field and to the lecture hall. There is almost no time to rest. Some people must think it is very hard, but we cannot make progress without hard work and patience. You all have jobs, and you have to take the time to receive a few months of training, and you must cherish these few months, so that you can live up to yourselves.

The Public Works Department Plans to Build a Prison in the Chinese Territory 137

A Request to the Consular Body to Handle

The Public Works Department Information Office announced yesterday that at a meeting of the Police Committee a few days ago, the Chief Patrol Officer submitted a report stating that the number of prisoners in the Western Prison on Huade Road has reached 7,046, and it is estimated that it will reach 7,500 by the end of the year. Not only is it crowded and worrying, but it is also feared that first-time offenders and minor offenders will be detained with serious criminals, which may lead to the contamination of bad habits. According to the current situation, if you want to detain prisoners according to the type of crime, it is impossible due to the situation. The only way to remedy the situation seems to be to designate the Western Prison on Huade Road to exclusively detain serious criminals with a sentence of more than two years, and build a new prison to detain minor criminals with a sentence of less than three years. It would be better if an agreement can be reached with the Chinese authorities to build a prison in the Chinese territory to detain minor criminals. In addition, the patrol room also manages prison administration, and the duties are too cumbersome. The Chief Patrol Officer is unable to take care of it. Whether it should be divided and a special office should be set up to be directly responsible to the Public Works Department should also be considered. After discussion by the members, the Public Works Department should be asked to consider it urgently. If it is difficult to add a new prison financially, the Consular Body should be asked to contact the Chinese authorities for the purpose of relief, and it is believed that if a new prison is built, it should be outside the concession. The Public Works Department should, in principle, agree that the number of prisoners detained in the Western Prison on Huade Road should not exceed 4,000. As for prison administration, it is agreed that the proposal of the Chief Patrol Officer will be followed. After Martin is back in Shanghai from his leave, he will be filled with the position of Extra Chief Patrol Officer, and Shanghai will be used as the warden of the prison. This case was submitted to the board's regular meeting on Wednesday for discussion. Because adding a new prison requires a lot of money, it was unanimously decided to ask the Consular Body to handle it as soon as possible according to the committee's recommendations.

Jardine Matheson's Jilong Wheel Explodes in Hong Kong 141

A Reuters dispatch from Hong Kong on the 15th reported that Jardine Matheson's Jilong (transliteration) ship suddenly exploded in its second cabin this morning while loading several barrels of cars next to the Mobil Oil Company's oil pool. The company's fire brigade and two fire boats from the Hong Kong government used water and chemicals to extinguish the fire in the cabin for two hours before the fire was put out, but the hull had already tilted 25 degrees to the left. Four workers are missing, and three others were seriously injured. Many workers were in the second cabin at the time, but they managed to escape, which was considered a miracle by everyone. One of them had a leg broken. The cause of the explosion has not yet been determined. The ship weighs 1,984 tons.

Dropping Prices to Compete is No Different From Suicide

Holding on to Monopoly Merchants Oppose

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Ping An, Yu He, Daxing, and other companies mutually opened Shanghai-Shashi regular ships, and the two sides brewed a big trend of shipping competition. Now, the Joint Shipping Bureau of the six companies has sent Bao Feng and Xin Renhe two ships to compete, and the fares have been greatly reduced, preparing to drop to free and then add gifts. Recently, the Bureau accused China Merchants of disrupting the situation to the Ministry of Communications, and the Ministry ordered the Shanghai Maritime Administration to investigate. Today, China Merchants submitted the details of the matter to the Maritime Administration, stating briefly that the company is a part of the China Merchants Bureau, and the profit and loss of its leased ships are related to the state-owned shipping industry. Moreover, with the smooth flow of highways, business is sluggish and it is difficult to maintain. Most routes have suspended classes. In order to adjust shipping, the Shanghai-Chongming and Shanghai-Shashi classes were added to make up for it. However, Zhang Housheng, the person in charge of the line, was not good at management, so the company took it back to operate on its own. Now it is greatly reorganized and strives to innovate, which is deeply welcomed by the people of Shanghai and Shashi. It is investigated that Shanghai-Shashi business is a legal business. How can there be speculation and intrusion to disrupt the situation? I don't know what the Bureau is based on. It is said that the Shanghai-Shashi Joint Shipping Bureau raised fares and monopolized profits. In June of this year, the gentry and merchants of Haimen were angry that they raised ship prices and held the shipping routes. They raised funds to create new wheels to maintain transportation. The Bureau's only plan is to hold on to the patent, which is a loss of the duty to serve the society. Moreover, the shipping routes are open, and each operates its business and is at peace. The Bureau is jealous of the same industry and must beat Jingde to the end. This case has been submitted to the Ministry to thoroughly investigate and stop it. Now the company preemptively accuses it of speculating and disrupting the situation. I don't know that Jingde wheel started sailing in April, and the Bureau was established in June. It was Jingde that started sailing first, and the Bureau was established later. Moreover, the Jingde fare is the same as the Bureau, but because there is no wharf, it is more than a dozen copper coins less to subsidize passengers' fares. On July 1, the Bureau made a big advertisement and arbitrarily reduced the fare, charging only 50%. The company was forced to do so and had to reduce the price according to the passengers' request. I think that dropping prices to compete is close to suicide. It is a pity to waste useful money on meaningless land. However, the dispute was opened by them, and the company could not reduce the price even if it did not want to. The Bureau only reduced the fare arbitrarily on the day Jingde opened (every other day), and raised the ship price again on the day Jingde did not sail, using the name of dropping the price to beat down Jingde on the one hand and deceiving passengers on the other hand. It used false economic power to overwhelm China Merchants and used sensational words to report to the Ministry to disrupt the situation as a word of resistance. If only the Bureau is allowed to sail on the Shanghai-Shashi line, then any shipping route can be arbitrarily held in the future. Moreover, Jingde applied to the competent authorities for approval at that time, which is also equivalent to a virtual setting. If it hinders the Bureau's shipping industry, it will lose the heart of the world for the public. The Bureau has been planning to trap Jingde in desperation, then Jingde can transfer to other lines, and other shipping bureaus can also use this to block shipping. I think that the disaster of competition is originally suspended as a severe prohibition. In case a tragedy is caused by the Bureau's price competition, the responsibility will be borne by the Bureau. (To be continued)

Three Doctors' Examination Procedures Not Completed

Trial Date Not Yet Determined

The results of the autopsy showed that there were no wounds on the body, and it was indeed a death from illness. However, due to the suspicion that the nasal cartilage had fallen off, the detached nasal bone was taken for expert research and examination to determine whether it was a new or old wound. It was originally scheduled that the three forensic doctors who came to the scene to examine the case that afternoon or the next day would issue an autopsy report and submit it to the court for approval. It has been repeatedly reported in the news. It is now learned that the forensic doctors have not completed the nasal bone examination procedures, so they have not discussed and decided, and the autopsy report has not been submitted to the court until yesterday morning. However, for the sake of caution, the court must wait for the autopsy report before it can set a trial date. Husband and Wife Accuse Each Other of an Embarrassing Photo 145

The Wife Accuses the Husband of Abandonment and Forcing to Sign a Note

The Husband Claims to Confirm the Divorce Contract

Gu Yuequan, a local who runs a furniture store at No. 38, Miaolong, English Concession, is 46 years old. In March of the 15th year of the Republic of China (lunar calendar), he married Zhou Huizhen (28 years old), a woman from this county, through a matchmaker. Since their marriage, the couple's feelings have been very strong for six years, and they have had three sons. Unexpectedly, they suddenly turned against each other. The husband accused his wife of adultery and had a divorce note. The wife accused her husband of doting on his concubine and bullying his wife, committing abuse, injuring her body, intending to abandon her, and forcing her to sign a note. They went to court and went to extremes. Gu hired lawyer Zhu Xiyi to sue his wife Zhou Huizhen in the civil court of the First Special District Court, requesting mediation to confirm the validity of the contract. The court hearing was held, but the mediation failed, so he officially filed a lawsuit.

The husband sues the wife. The plaintiff's wife, Zhou Huizhen, committed adultery with Shan Yonglin. On June 9, the plaintiff arrested them both in room 6 of the Datong Hotel on Six Ma Road. At that time, they were handed over to the patrol room and sent to the court for investigation. Later, the defendant asked Dong Xinhai to come to persuade them, saying that the defendant was aware of committing adultery and violating the morals of women, and was now willing to sign a divorce note for each party to use as evidence. Unexpectedly, the plaintiff recently entrusted lawyer Cai Xiaobai to publish a notice denying the divorce and falsely accusing the plaintiff of forcing the note. It is found that Shan and the defendant committed adultery, and there is full evidence. The publication of the denial is obviously intended to renege, so he specially filed a lawsuit, requesting that the divorce contract signed by the plaintiff and defendant on June 9 be confirmed as valid. The court president Zhou Han came to the seventh court to hear the case on the morning of the day before yesterday. The defendant Zhou Huizhen was not present. According to the plaintiff Gu Yuequan's confession, he ran into his wife and Shan walking together in the French Concession on June 9, so he followed them and witnessed them entering room 6 of the Datong Hotel and saw Zhou and Shan together in bed through the window outside the room. So he waited until the next morning before he went to arrest the adultery, and there was a photo taken at the time as evidence, so he submitted the case. The photo showed a man and a woman sitting on the bed. The man was only wearing a small shirt, and the woman was barefoot and only wearing a shirt and pants. The situation was very embarrassing. Later, court president Zhou said that the defendant could not be found, so he ordered the notice to be served and then verified. This is the situation of the husband suing the wife.

The wife sues the husband. However, Zhou Huizhen also hired lawyer Tao Wuzhi to file a lawsuit, accusing her husband Gu Yuequan, Shan Yonglin, Dong Xinhai, etc. of abuse, injury, and forced signing of a note in the criminal court of the Special Court. Yesterday morning, judge Ge Shixun came to the criminal court to gather information. Only the defendant Gu Yuequan and his lawyer were present. Shan and Dong were not present. Zhou Huizhen, the self-accuser, confessed that after marrying the defendant, she had three sons and the relationship was harmonious. Three years later, Gu gradually developed the idea of abandoning the old and liking the new, and took Zhang Lanbao as his concubine. At about 9 pm on April 16 this year, due to a trivial matter, the defendant immediately stabbed my left hand with a knife, causing serious injuries and bleeding profusely. Fortunately, she met a Chinese patrol on the way and sent her to Renji Hospital for treatment, and reported to the General Patrol Room. The patrol officer said that since it was a husband and wife relationship, it was inconvenient to interfere and told her to file a lawsuit in court. The defendant Gu Yuequan was deeply afraid that I would formally file a lawsuit, so he changed his methods to deal with me, pretending to reconcile with me, and secretly designing to frame me. On the evening of June 9 this year, he said that the weather was stuffy and borrowed a hotel to stay in for comfort. I believed it to be true and went to live in the Datong Hotel on Six Ma Road. The next morning at 9 o'clock, Gu made an excuse to go out to collect debts. At 11 o'clock, the bastard Shan Yonglin broke into the room. When I asked about his intentions, before I could finish a word, more than a dozen hooligans followed in, holding pistols, with a fierce momentum, claiming to arrest adultery as a reason, forcing me and Shan to be adulterers and adulteresses, and Shan did not argue about this point, and remained silent. At this time, even if I had a hundred mouths, it would be difficult to explain. While arguing, Gu Yuequan, a photographer, and a lawyer entered the room together, forced me to take a photo with Shan, and ordered Shan to take off his clothes. If there was any resistance, they would use fists and feet and aim the pistol to shoot. Under this circumstance, I completely lost my freedom. A man named Dong Xinhai, who claimed to be Lu Zhongda, acted as a mediator and pretended to persuade me. Then the lawyer drafted a single contract to break away from the husband and wife relationship and forced me to sign the contract. Shan and Dong actually acted as witnesses. I was unwilling to sign, and the hooligans pointed at me with pistols, saying that if I did not sign, I would be executed immediately. After signing, they took me to the pre-hired car to Lawyer Wu's office and copied several copies of the single contract, and then forced me to sign it before I could escape from the tiger's den. I now live in my mother's home in Longji Lane, North Zhejiang Road, so I specially came to file a lawsuit. Judge Ge verified the confession and learned that the plaintiff Zhou Huizhen and the defendant Gu Yuequan were formally married. According to Article 339 of the Criminal Procedure Law, formal spouses may not self-accuse and must be filed by the patrol room. He then explained this to the plaintiff's lawyer Tao Wuzhi and instructed him to convey it to the plaintiff. After the instructions were completed, he wrote on the case dismissal form that this case would not be accepted.

Zhang Wenming, the owner of Songmaoyuan Paper Store at Nos. 53-54 Shandong Road and a native of Wuxi, 45 years old, returned with his wife from a relative's house at 3 am yesterday morning. Zhang saw the situation and knew that they were not good people, so he told his wife to give him the cigarette holder and shouted "Robber" wildly. The robbers were afraid that the patrolmen would come, so they hurriedly pulled out a gun and fired a shot, hitting his left heel. Blood was pouring out. The robbers fled into the horizontal lane. Verification of the Death of Two People Run Over by an American Military Vehicle 156

On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, around 3 PM, Zhou Zhengfu (age 28) and Tian Laihai (age 36), two rickshaw pullers from Jiangbei, were resting by the roadside at the intersection of South Suzhou Road and Yuanmingyuan Road due to the hot weather. Unexpectedly, a military truck with license plate number 9814, carrying more than 20 Navy personnel from the American military camp at 50 Haifang Road, was speeding eastward from the park's shooting range towards the Moore Road barracks. The driver, an American soldier named Ker-Ai-Er Chi-Si (transliteration), struck Zhou and Tian, causing severe injuries. A Chinese patrolman from post number 39 witnessed the incident, immediately recorded the truck's license plate number, and transported the two injured men by car to Renji Hospital. They succumbed to their injuries and died shortly after. The incident was reported to the General Inspectorate, which ordered detectives to investigate. The bodies were then transported to the autopsy station on Fielun Road. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court appointed Prosecutor Zhang Yaoguang, along with medical examiner Zhang Junrun, clerk Wang Zuyi, and others, to the station to examine the bodies. Driver Ker-Ai-Er Chi-Si, age 26, American, stated that while driving through the intersection of South Suzhou Road and Yuanmingyuan Road, he saw a car of unknown license plate stopped in the middle of the road. He attempted to steer slightly south to avoid the car, but it suddenly moved. At that moment, there was a damaged vehicle and two rickshaws parked on the south side of the road. The two deceased were standing next to the rickshaws, causing his vehicle to collide with the damaged vehicle. The damaged vehicle was pushed by his car and then collided with the rickshaws, resulting in the injuries of the two men. He stated that his car did not directly hit them. Pan A'san and Shen Jiufu testified that they were pulling rickshaws with Zhou and Tian. At the time, they stopped to rest by the roadside because of the long distance and hot weather. There was a damaged vehicle parked in front of their two rickshaws. Zhou and Tian were securing the goods on their rickshaws when the military truck sped from the west, first colliding with the damaged vehicle, then violently colliding with their two rickshaws, causing them to overturn and injuring Zhou and Tian. Zhang Jun obtained the statements and ruled that the deceased, Zhou Zhengfu and Tian Laihai, died as a result of being run over by vehicle number 9814. The bodies were handed over to Pushan Villa for funeral arrangements.

Armed Fight on Guohuo Road 157

Many Severely Injured

Huang Yaxiang, Cai Ruihua, Cai Guochu, and others, residents of Guohuo Road in the South City, are known to be troublemakers. A dispute arose between women over two roots of vegetables. They attempted to resolve the matter at a small teahouse at the entrance of Nandeshengli, but to no avail. Immediately, they engaged in a major armed fight on the street with iron rods, axes, single-edged swords, and handguns. As a result, Huang Yaxiang, Huang Hu, Li Donggui, Xiao Meichu, Chen Ziyun, Li Zhenyuan, Li Zhenfu, and others were severely injured. Some had head wounds with blood and brain matter flowing out, others had ruptured abdomens with intestines spilling out. All were in life-threatening condition. The police from the Chezhan Road Police Station arrived and took the injured to the Second District. They were immediately presented to the District Court, where the prosecutor examined them and sent them to Xin Puyu Hall for treatment. After the bloody battle concluded, three cars arrived at Guohuo Road at 6 PM, and over thirty people wearing white shirts and black pants jumped out. Each was armed with a handgun and searched Guohuo Road for the residents who had fought that morning. However, all of them had fled and hidden, so a major disaster was narrowly avoided. Residents of Guohuo Road, who were outside enjoying the evening breeze, saw the situation and rushed indoors, closing their doors to avoid trouble, suffering a scare.

Viciousness of Adulterers 158

Fearing the Concubine Would Report to Her Husband

They Defiled Her As Well

The Affair Was Exposed, and They Fled Together

Lu Yunsheng, a 37-year-old platoon leader in the Shanghai City Defense Corps from Zhenjiang, resided at 83 Jiaxing Road, Hongkou. The upstairs was his home, and the downstairs was Lu Yun Ji Paint Shop, which Lu owned. Lu had a wife and a concubine. The wife, Tang Zhenzhu, was 29 years old and had been married for 12 years. The concubine, Zhang Dongqin, was only 18 and had been married for just six months. They all lived together. Tang, while not beautiful, was extremely promiscuous and had an ongoing affair with Li Zhifa (age 23) from Pudong, who worked at the shop. They had been secretly meeting for some time. However, they were constrained by Lu's presence and could not fully indulge. Recently, Lu fell ill and resided alone in the attic, leaving his wife and concubine in the front building. On the night of the 9th of this month, Tang saw that Zhang was sound asleep and invited Li upstairs to meet again. As they were finishing, Zhang suddenly woke up. Tang and Li, realizing their affair was exposed and fearing that Zhang would report to Lu Yunsheng, decided to silence her. Tang covered Zhang's mouth, while Li straddled her and forcibly raped her. Their intention was to prevent Zhang from speaking out, believing that if she was defiled, she would be too ashamed to reveal the truth. However, after being defiled, Zhang immediately told her husband. Tang and Li, realizing their plan had failed and they could no longer stay at Lu's house, packed up over a thousand yuan worth of clothing and ornaments and fled together. Lu reported the incident to the Hongkou Police Station, which dispatched detectives Bao Shuji, Bao Liu Decheng, and Mu Chunrong to investigate Lu's home. They found Li Zhifa's cigarette case under Tang's pillow and a bundle of soiled cloth and Li's clothing under the bed, which they took back to the police station. The evening before last, around 12 AM, Detective Bao and others learned that Tang and Li were hiding in room 45 of the Si Ming Xie Ji Hotel at 96 West Zilaihuo Street in the French Concession, using the names Wang Kechang and Wang Lushi. They coordinated with detectives from the French Police to raid the room, arresting the adulterers. They also recovered a suitcase containing the items Tang had taken. They were taken back to the police station and detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were transferred to the Criminal Court of the First Special District, where Judge Huang Weihua opened the court for questioning. The police station's lawyer, Hu Jiabao, stated that due to the urgency of the case, the police station had not yet formally filed charges and requested permission for temporary detention. Detective Bao then gave a report on the circumstances of the case. Tang Zhenzhu denied the affair with Li, claiming that Zhang Dongqin had falsely accused her. Li Zhifa did not deny the affair with Tang. Judge Huang ordered the two defendants to be detained and adjourned the case for further investigation before submitting it for trial.

The Domestic Goods Association Introduces Domestic Steel Reeds 174

The Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of Domestic Goods has repeatedly received letters from domestic goods factories in this city and other cities producing silk, satin, cloth, and various cotton textiles, stating that they all use enemy goods from the small character brand for their required steel reeds. Since the September 18th Incident and the invasion of Northeast China, the people of the whole country have been angered and are enthusiastically boycotting enemy goods. Those with substitutes have stopped using them and are actively manufacturing domestic goods, striving to save the situation. However, the steel reed is an essential item for this industry. Shanghai is a concentrated area for the production of domestic goods. They are requesting the association to investigate whether domestic products are available for purchase, or to encourage their creation, in order to facilitate boycotts. The association believes that the demand for steel reeds is extremely high, with each industry losing over洋2 million. Promoting domestic goods and increasing production is a bulwark against enemy goods and a long-term tool for resistance. The association has a responsibility to investigate and cannot decline. The association assigned the investigation to the investigation section. It is now known that investigation section members Chen Binghui and Yang Yucheng have been working hard in the summer heat and have found the following four factories in Shanghai that manufacture and supply steel reeds: (1) China Steel Reed Factory, Gong character trademark, factory located at the Tianhou Palace Bridge approach; (2) Shanghai Steel Reed Factory, Xiang character trademark, factory located in Heng'an Lane, Nanyang Bridge; (3) Wulin Steel Reed Factory, Double Ten trademark, factory located in Huaxing Lane, Tangshan Road; (4) Qinyi Steel Reed Factory, Yi character trademark, factory located in Sanxing Lane, Baoding Road. The products are of good quality and are no less than enemy goods, and the prices are also lower. Moreover, the production volume is extremely high and sufficient for the application of domestic goods factories, making them a vital force in the production of domestic goods. The association has already sent letters and steel reed samples from each factory to those who requested it for trial use, and has also notified factories in various industries that require this product to promote cooperation.
